The World's Eyes Focus on Rome

The Italian-Austrian-Hungarian Tripartite Conference Begins

The Surface Focus is on Economic and Commercial Affairs

In Reality, It is to Unite Against Germany

The Conference Will Seek to Expand and Enlist the Small Entente Countries to Join

It is Rumored That Germany Plans to Build a New Canal to Undermine Italian Policy

Rome Since today, Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss and Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös have been formally invited by the Italian government and treated as state guests. Dollfuss will hold his first meeting with Prime Minister Mussolini at noon today. Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös and former Austrian Deputy Chancellor Winkler will begin working together at 10:00 this morning. After meeting with Dollfuss, Gömbös will meet with the German Ambassador to Italy. At noon, Prince Sheqi will host a banquet, which will be attended by all important figures from Austria and Hungary in Rome. (14th Day Havas Dispatch)

Austrian Prime Minister Declares Independence

Rome Before the start of the tripartite conference here today, Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss told guests that Italy, Austria, and Hungary are now trying to prevent the Danube countries from engaging in mutually destructive struggles, which would exhaust their strength. Austria's duty is to reconcile the Danube countries and unite them. To achieve this goal, Austria must maintain its autonomy and independence, which has been proven by recent events. This morning, the Austrian Prime Minister held lengthy discussions with the Italian Prime Minister, and then engaged in discussions with the Hungarian Prime Minister. It is heard that Austria wants to obtain satisfactory conditions for using Trieste as a maritime outlet, and wants to increase the sales of Austrian timber in Italy. (14th Day Reuters Dispatch)

Rome The Italian-Hungarian-Austrian conference, which is related to the security of the political situation and world peace, opened here today. The cabinet ministers of the three countries arrived one after another to conduct discussions on the critical situation between Germany and Austria. 100,000 Italian troops are stationed on the Austrian border today, ready to repel any enemy that invades the two countries at any time. Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania are also prepared to fight in the event of an incident. The meeting of Prime Minister Mussolini of Italy, Prime Minister Dollfuss of Austria, and Prime Minister Gömbös of Hungary in Rome today will determine the actions taken by the three countries in the face of the German National Socialist Party's endangering Austria, in order to realize the agreement between the three countries. A communiqué issued by the secretariat of the conference stated that the purpose of this conference is to discuss the economic relations between the three countries, but it is believed that the main topic of the meeting is the policy related to the situation in Germany and Austria. Prime Minister Mussolini spoke first, requesting the abandonment of rhetoric on political action, and turning to discussing strengthening Austria's position to resist the National Socialist Party's conspiracy to occupy it, in order to avoid war. Prime Minister Mussolini expressed his disgust with military disarmament trends and European political negotiations, and declared that he personally would try to save the crisis in Central Europe. Before departing for Rome, Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss made an important adjustment to the cabinet, in order to strengthen the power of the royalists to suppress the National Socialist Party, and to slightly suppress the unrest elements in Austria. Prince Hatton has now been appointed as Minister of Defense. Given the current situation in Austria, the Minister of Defense is the most important position in the Austrian government. This position was previously held concurrently by Prime Minister Dollfuss. (13th Day National Telegram)

Related to the Future of Central Europe

Rome The Prime Ministers of Austria and Hungary have come here together to discuss important matters related to the future of Central Europe with the Italian authorities. Therefore, the eyes of the world are now focused on Rome, and no European leader is not closely watching the development of the situation here.

Britain and France Closely Watch

At the same time, Reuters learned that the British government fully expressed its sympathy, only needing to avoid dangerous political disputes. The French government feels that the revitalization of the Danube basin is beneficial to the matter. This attitude may make the Little Entente countries view the Rome talks with a friendly eye.

The Austrian Prime Minister is Overwhelmed by Favor

When Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss arrived in Rome last night, the welcome ceremony was extremely grand. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and many dignitaries personally went to greet him, and when the Austrian Prime Minister drove to the official residence, it was almost a triumphal procession. The crowds in the streets were as thick as walls, and the cheers continued. The Austrian Prime Minister seemed not to have expected such honor, and raised his hand to give a Fascist salute in response.

The Three Countries Submit Memorandums to Each Other

Negotiations begin today with the aim of establishing an economic alliance. If successful, the European future will have far-reaching political implications, and not just economic ones. The Italian, Austrian, and Hungarian sides have submitted memoranda as the basis for talks. The Italian memorandum is based on the recommendations of the Stresa Conference (which opened in 1932, with fifteen countries discussing the financial and economic transformation of Central and Eastern Europe), advocating the conclusion of bilateral economic and regional agreements.

Difficult Commercial Issues

The Hungarian Prime Minister arrived here on Sunday and has already discussed commercial issues with the Italian Prime Minister, especially focusing on Italian-Hungarian freight rates. This is a thorny issue, as Hungary's exports are mostly rice and livestock, while Italy does not need rice and can purchase cheaper livestock from Yugoslavia, as Yugoslavia is closer to Italy. Similar difficulties will also be encountered between Italy and Austria, as Italy is best suited to trade with Yugoslavia due to natural conditions, while Austria is best suited to trade with Czechoslovakia. Therefore, Italy is eager to expand the scope of its meetings and enlist the three Small Entente countries, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania, to join the conference.

Czechoslovakia Softens Towards Italy

Czechoslovakia has recently softened its attitude towards Italy, but is still unwilling to shake hands with Italy immediately. However, it is rumored that Czech Foreign Minister Beneš is now willing to meet with the Italian Prime Minister to explain everything.

Determination to Aid Austrian Independence

It is generally believed that the meeting of the Prime Ministers of Italy, Austria, and Hungary will not involve the difficult issue of the restoration of the Austrian imperial system. The Small Entente countries have made it clear that they will regard Austria's restoration as an act that would lead to an immediate declaration of war. It is generally recognized that the main purpose of the Italian Prime Minister is to maintain Austria's independence, as the European balance of power would be disrupted if Austria were under German control. Austria lost a lot of land due to the Treaty of Trianon and now wants to gain Italy's assistance to extend its demand for amending this treaty and other unfavorable treaties.

Germany Plots Destruction

It is rumored that German Chancellor Hitler has now devised a clever plan to undermine Austria's increasingly friendly relationship with Italy, planning to build a canal connecting the Danube and Elbe Rivers to avoid the Italian Prime Minister enticing Austria and Hungary with the outlet to the Adriatic Sea through Trieste and Fiume. If the plan to build this canal is implemented, the Danube River's commerce will shift to Germany, and Germany's superior position in Central Europe will be further established. (14th Day Reuters Dispatch)

Military Disarmament is Reaching a Dead End

The French Reply to the British Note Will be Sent Out Today

Will Clearly Reject the British Proposal

Britain Attempts to Convene an Air Force Conference

To Open Up New Paths for Military Disarmament

(Paris) According to news today, France's note to Britain on Thursday will clearly declare the failure of military disarmament negotiations and open up new paths to seek practical discussions on military disarmament. The recent British memorandum on military disarmament to various European countries, as well as the United States and Japan, is Britain's last effort for the "months-long stalemate of the military disarmament crisis." After being studied by the French National Defense Council, the French reply has been formally drafted. The note reiterates the reasons why France cannot accept the British plan and details why France cannot disarm, as Germany demands the restoration of arms. France and Germany are neighboring countries, and Germany is warlike, so how can France disarm and rest easy? According to French political sources, the British government had expected France to reject its proposal and knows that the British government is now planning to invite the world's major powers to participate in an air force conference to seek a new way out for military disarmament. The location of the conference is rumored to be London. Britain believes that the status of its own air force is still very dangerous, so it believes that the British air force must be equal to the air force military strength of any other country (that is capable of attacking Britain). British-Japanese Textile Industry Negotiations

Formally Declared Ruptured Yesterday

Japan Rejects New British Proposal

Future Negotiations to Be Handled by the Government

Britain Disagrees on Abolishing the Trade Treaty

(London) The British-Japanese textile industry conference has now broken down. Today, representatives from both sides held a joint meeting, then withdrew from the meeting place for a private meeting, and finally announced the breakdown of negotiations. The Japanese delegation was instructed by the Osaka Cotton Spinning Association to terminate negotiations if the British side did not change its attitude towards the scope of the region. The failure of today's talks was due to this instruction. The British chief representative decided today to ask the government to handle the matter. The British chief representative, Mr. Barlow, stated today that he does not know what the Japanese side will do. The basis put forward by the Japanese side is unacceptable to the British side, and the British side's demands are unacceptable to the Japanese side. The Japanese side now claims that the current position is hopeless. The memorandum submitted by the British side to the Japanese delegation has been published, containing specific suggestions as follows: (1) The British representatives agree to discuss starting from one or more regions, and the Japanese representatives can choose this region. The requested designated regions are Africa, Asia, the Near East, the Middle East, Europe, South America, and Central America. (2) The markets included in the Near East and the Middle East are not included in Asia or Europe. (3) The markets within the British Empire and the Japanese Empire must be regarded as separate regions, and they will be discussed after considerable progress has been made in the discussion of other regions. (4) The discussion of each region does not hinder the freedom of the representatives of both sides to form their entire final resolution. Today, members of the House of Commons asked the government what actions it would take regarding the breakdown of the negotiations. Under-Secretary of State for Overseas Self-Government Malcolm MacDonald replied that this was not something he could answer. We are prepared to support the negotiations to achieve success. Members also asked what actions the Colonial Office would take regarding Japanese goods. Malcolm MacDonald replied that this question should be answered at a later date. (Reuters telegram, 14th)

(Tokyo) According to reliable sources, Japanese textile industry leaders today telegraphed the Japanese delegation in London, stating that if the British proposals regarding regions and quantities can be implemented, it may be possible to continue negotiations. This move indicates that Japan wants to establish an agreement with Britain and its territories first, and then involve other regions. Japan refuses to acknowledge unilateral restrictions and reductions in any case. It is reported that the Japanese government has no intention of intervening at the moment. The British-Japanese cotton industry talks are scheduled to continue today. (Reuters telegram, 14th)

(London) The Japanese cotton industry representatives visited Mr. Matsudaira, the British Ambassador, on the afternoon of the 13th, and explained in detail the reasons why they had to reject the British proposal regarding the British-Japanese conference. They also said that if the British side does not change its attitude, the conference on the 14th will have no other solution than a breakdown, and they hope to be understood. Ambassador Matsudaira hoped that even if the negotiations were to break down out of necessity, they should still be concluded satisfactorily in order to reserve room for the resumption of future conferences. (Jiji News Agency telegram, 14th)

(London) The British and Japanese cotton textile industry conference suddenly declared a breakdown today. The opinions of the representatives from both sides are quite different, and it is feared that it will be difficult for both sides to reconcile without the intervention of diplomats. The British side is currently paying close attention to the British-Japanese trade treaty signed in 1868, and there is concern that this will lead to a commercial war between Britain and Japan. However, opinions within Britain are also quite divided. One group of people advocates maintaining the old trade treaty, while another group strongly advocates abolishing the trade treaty. In recent years, British cotton textile, rubber, and porcelain merchants have suffered greatly from competition from Japanese merchants, so they deeply hope that the trade treaty can be abolished as soon as possible. However, general postal companies, chemical plants, and steel machinery plants are reluctant to abolish this trade treaty because their sales in Japan are quite good, which would hurt the feelings of British and Japanese businessmen. According to the speculation of general banking personnel, they feel that Japan has long-term debts of about 150 million Japanese yen in the London market. Once the trade treaty is abolished, it will have a significant impact on such debts, so the banking industry also opposes the proposal to abolish the trade treaty. (National News Agency telegram, 14th)

Iraq Boycotts Japanese Goods

Marseille. A Syrian newspaper sent from Beirut (Syria) was received here today, reporting news from the capital of Iraq, saying that the Iraqi people have begun to express dissatisfaction with the import of Japanese manufactured goods. For example, the people of Shatra and Nahlwa Sli recently held demonstrations against merchants selling Japanese goods, surrounding the stores of these merchants, resulting in significant losses. After this movement, the Iraqi government seems to have decided to increase the import tax on Japanese goods, and an order will be issued soon to implement it. According to the same news, the import of British Lancashire goods into Iraq decreased by 62% compared to previous years, while the import of Japanese goods increased by 23%. (Havas telegram, 13th)

Japanese Torpedo Boat Disaster

57 Bodies Recovered

Sorrow Shrouds Sasebo

Anger Directed at Naval Treaty

Sasebo. As of 4:30 PM, the rescue work for Tomozuru had discovered the bodies of nine people, including First Class Engineer Eguchi Yutaro. To date, a total of fifty-seven bodies have been found. (Dentsu telegram, 14th)

Sasebo. The drainage and rescue work for the torpedo boat Tomozuru is not only a desperate effort by all members through the night, but also officers and employees are making noises by hitting iron plates with iron hammers to add energy to the survivors inside the boat. Starting at 0:50 AM on the 14th, they began to chisel holes in the bottom of the boat. Fearing the intrusion of evil gas into the boat, they did not use acetylene gas, but continued to cut the iron plates with a furnace. At 1:50 AM, they rescued Petty Officer Third Class Yanagida Suteichi and one sailor and accommodated them in the naval hospital. At 2:00 AM, they made full contact with the inside of the boat. As a result of the rescue team's search inside the boat, they carried out thirteen bodies of victims and placed them in the Hubei War Memorial Hall. At 2:30 AM, they discovered Petty Officer Third Class Inoue Heiji and Tajima Sanmori, both unconscious and collapsed inside the boat. Petty Officer Tajima eventually died. At 5:30 AM, they found the bodies of three sailors and placed them in the memorial hall. At the same time, for the sake of rescue, two holes have been opened. At 6:00 AM, there was no response to external questions. Officers and soldiers below the commander showed more concern. The rescue team continued their silent work. As of now, in addition to the rescued and the 31 dead who have been carried out, there are still 83 people who may still be trapped inside the boat, but their fate is hopeless. More than 300 family members of the crew are hugging each other and crying every time the names of survivors are announced.

No officer below the rank of Sa has been found. These officers are probably all on the bridge directing, and were swept away by the waves when they capsized. Among those who have been identified as dead, the names of petty officers second class and above are as follows: Petty Officer Second Class Atsumoto Yoshio, Nagao Heihati, Petty Officer Third Class Koga Shigeru. (Dentsu telegram, 14th)

Sasebo. Admiral Suetsugu, Commander of the Combined Fleet, said about the Tomozuru disaster: Although Tomozuru does not belong to the Combined Fleet, it is a newly built elite torpedo boat, not to be compared with the torpedo boats at the time of the Russo-Japanese War. It is strange that such a new type of warship should capsize. There was a big storm at sea that night. Waves washed over the deck of such a huge battleship "Kongo" like a waterfall. Tomozuru is a small boat of 527 tons, and it is expected that maneuvering will be difficult. Japan builds such defensive warships because of the restrictions of the naval treaty. Japan has to advocate abolishing proportionalism and establishing equality of armaments. (Jiji News Agency telegram, 14th)

(London) The Manchester Guardian commented on the loss of the Japanese torpedo boat Tomozuru, saying that it was caused by the excessive weight of the cannons installed on the boat. The newspaper said that the Tomozuru incident is not trivial. In the future, similar naval boats will inevitably be modified due to this incident. According to reports, the Tomozuru has a displacement of only 527 tons, but carries as many as three 5-inch caliber cannons. Compared with similar British torpedo destroyers, the Tomozuru carries too much cannon. The British torpedo destroyer Akaste has a displacement of 1,350 tons and carries only four 4.7-inch caliber cannons. (Havas News Agency telegram, 14th)

Svanør Steamer Completely Destroyed

(Hong Kong) The steamer Svanør of the Douglas Steamship Company ran aground near Fuzhou on Sunday and has now been completely destroyed. Rescue was ineffective. (Reuters telegram, 14th)

Trade Policy Towards Russia

State-Owned Enterprises Not Easy to Implement

(Nanjing) After the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, our country planned to establish state-owned enterprises for trade with Russia in order to control it and avoid unilateral dumping. However, the state-owned enterprise plan has two problems. First, the Chinese people's free trade has become a habit, and second, the advantages and disadvantages of the state-owned method are mutually evident. If we want to prevent unilateral dumping, the current situation of dumping is not unique to Russia. The situation in other countries is the same. Therefore, the Ministry of Industry believes that it is not easy to start a state-owned enterprise plan solely for Russia and has to change its policy. The responsible authorities are studying in detail the cooperative policy between the government and merchants in order to adapt to customs and ensure consistency in trade with various countries. (Special telegram, 14th)

Four-Route Army

Will Soon Encircle and Suppress Jiangxi Bandits

Bandit Areas Only Include Thirteen Counties in Jiangxi and Fujian

Fujian Provincial Government Sends Personnel to Count and Organize People's Militia

Xiamen correspondence: Since Chiang Ting-wen returned from Guangdong, the four-route army's encirclement and suppression of Jiangxi bandits is about to be realized. Sun Yuanliang, Leng Xin, Chen Mingren, Lu Xingbang, and other divisions in northern Fujian captured Jiangle County on the 7th. The bandit Fang Zhimin's forces retreated to Tai Ning. Currently, the communist bandits in northern Fujian have completely failed. In western Fujian, the 3rd Division of the 4th Column of the Central Army took over defense of Longyan on the 7th. Fan Ling's supplementary regiment of the division is now stationed in Longyan City. A small part of the 1st Independent Division of the Guangdong Army under Huang Renhuan, Yan Yingyu's brigade, which was originally stationed in the city, withdrew at noon on the 7th, heading to Yongding Kanshi via Nanyang Dam. Peng Guozhen, the magistrate of Longyan County appointed by the Guangdong Army, also went with the army. The 3rd Division is expected to arrive in Yan in full on the 10th. Division Commander Li Yutang is also scheduled to depart for Yan on the 10th. Li Chuying's 247th Brigade of the 83rd Division under Liu Kan arrived in Zhangzhou on the 8th. The 249th Brigade and the supplementary regiment arrived in Tong'an on the 8th and are expected to reach Zhangzhou on the 10th or 11th. The division is also preparing to advance on Longyan, with the 9th Division as a reserve force, remaining in Zhangzhou for replenishment and training. According to military intelligence, the area currently occupied by Jiangxi bandits is limited to the area from Guangchang and Luo Chang in the north to Huichang and Junmenling in the south, from Xingguo in the west to Ninghua in Fujian in the east, accounting for only seven counties in Jiangxi: Guangchang, Shicheng, Ningdu, Xingguo, Yudu, Ruijin, and Huichang. And six counties in Fujian: Tai Ning, Jian Ning, Ninghua, Guihua, Liancheng, and Changting, totaling thirteen counties. The main force is mostly in the Guangchang and Tai Ning area. Only local communists are in Liancheng, and only a small number of red bandits are in Changting. After the Fujian Rebellion was quelled, the National Army resumed strict blockades, and the shortage of edible salt in the bandit areas has become increasingly severe. It is predictable that they cannot withstand the four-route army's encirclement and suppression, leading to their extermination.

Besides suppressing bandits, the only problem in Fujian Province is the aftermath of the people's militia, especially the people's militia in southern Fujian, whose numbers account for more than 80% of the province's people's militia. Xiao Jing, director of the western and southern Fujian security branch, passed through Xiamen to Quanzhou on the 3rd of this month to first inspect the Quanzhou-Yongchun-Xingren people's militia and to determine the counting and organization procedures. On the 6th, he counted and organized Ma Hongxing's troops. On the 7th, he counted and organized Chen Peiyu's troops. On the 9th, he counted and organized Lin Jing's troops in Xianyou. On the 10th, he counted and organized Chen Yucai's troops in Anxi. On the 12th, he counted and organized Peng Tang's troops in Yongchun. After counting, Ma Hongxing's troops had more than 700 guns and more than ten machine guns. The guns were all qualified. After Chen Peiyu's troops were counted, more than 1,000 qualified guns were found. The results of Lin Jing's troops' count are not yet known. In addition, Liu Chaoran also applied to the southern district security branch on the 8th to be counted, and Zhang Xiongnan also applied for a count. Both are awaiting a scheduled count. The war between Hong Wende and Zhang Xiongnan has been stopped in accordance with the Provincial Government's telegram order and ceased fire on the 4th. Zhang is based in Dehua, and Hong is based in Yongchun. Xiao Jing spoke to news reporters in Quanzhou on the 8th, roughly saying that the Provincial Government has limited the people's militia in the province to seven regiments in principle. It has been decided to organize the people's militia in southern Fujian into five regiments. The first phase counts and organizes Hong Wende (Peng Tang, Chen Peiyu, Chen Yucai, Liu Chaoran are all included), Zhang Xiongnan, Lin Jing and other troops belonging to Quanzhou, Yongchun, and Xingren. The second phase counts and organizes Yang Fengnian's troops belonging to Zhangzhou. The third phase counts various people's militia in western Fujian. The organization of the people's militia takes the regiment as the highest unit, named "Fujian Provincial Security Team, Number X Regiment," according to the infantry organization. Below the regiment are battalions and companies. Each company is limited to 90 guns. The standard for counting is guns. Foreign-made, Hanyang-made, and Guangdong-made guns are considered qualified. Min-made, short guns, and miscellaneous guns are not qualified. After counting, the second step is to organize the committee, the third step is to organize training, and the fourth step is to transfer the garrison. The remaining people's militia will either have their guns purchased and be dismissed, or be dealt with in other appropriate ways. The salaries of the security team will be issued by the provincial treasury and will no longer be obtained from other sources. The Bao Wei Tuan is funded locally. Currently, the provincial government has decided to allocate 180,000 yuan per month from foreign rice tax for security regiment expenses. In addition, Xiao Qian, deputy director of the Provincial Security Department, flew from the province to Xiamen on the 7th. Xiao Jing came to Xiamen from Quanzhou on the same day to meet Xiao Qian, asking for instructions on counting the people's militia in Quanzhou. Xiao Qian then went to Zhangzhou on the 8th and to Nanjing on the 9th to inspect Yang Fengnian's people's militia, summoning officers above the rank of major for training. He returned to Zhangzhou in the afternoon. According to Zhangzhou military intelligence, Yang Fengnian's troops will be organized into three regiments and four independent battalions, with each regiment having twelve infantry companies (each company with 81 guns), one machine gun company, one mortar company, one medical team, and one communications platoon. According to news from Yang Fengnian, the regimental and battalion commanders have been appointed, but they have not been formally counted by the Provincial Government, so the Provincial Government has not appointed them. (March 10)

Zhang Xueliang Returns to Hankou

—Plans for Bandit Suppression and Aftermath Determined in Jiangxi—

—Scheduled to Summon and Train Generals Arriving in Hankou—

Hankou Correspondence: Zhang Xueliang, Deputy Commander of the Bandit Suppression for the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, accompanied by Shen Honglie and He Zhuguo, took the Wuxue steamer to Xunyang on the 7th. On the morning of the 8th, they changed to a special train on the Nanxun Road to the south, arriving in Nanchang at 2:00 PM. He spent several days consulting with Chairman Chiang on the aftermath of bandit suppression in the three provinces, deciding on concrete plans. At 12:00 PM on the afternoon of the 12th, Zhang and others departed from Nanchang to return to Hankou. They arrived in Xunyang at 8:00 AM on the 13th and immediately boarded the Yong Sui warship with staff members Tang Guozhen, Tan Hai, Li Tiancai, and He Wenxu to sail upstream. Shen Honglie and He Zhuguo took another merchant ship westward. The Yong Sui warship arrived in Hankou at 10:30 PM on the afternoon of the 13th, docking at the Sanbei pier. He Chengjuan, Wan Fulin, Wang Yizhe, Qian Dagou, Zeng Yiding, Ye Peng, and the division commanders from the Northeast who came to Hankou, Liu Duoquan, Liu Handong, Guo Xipeng, Dong Yingbin, Zhang Decheng, and Zhu Hongxun, all welcomed him at the wharf. After disembarking, Zhang went to the headquarters to rest. Due to the fatigue of the journey, Tang Guozhen was specially sent to meet the reporters. According to him, Mr. Zhang's trip to Jiangxi lasted a week. He met with Chairman Chiang every day in Nanchang. Concrete plans have been made regarding future military affairs and the aftermath of bandit suppression in the three provinces. After returning to Hankou, he may go to the bandit area for inspection, but the time cannot be predetermined. The rumor that a headquarters will be established in Hankou is definitely not true. The generals from North China who were summoned to Jiangxi by telegram from Chiang have been concentrated in Beiping and are heading south. Those who arrived in Hankou on the 13th include: Huang Jie, commander of the Second Division, Liu Handong, commander of the 107th Division, Liu Duoquan, commander of the 105th Division, Guo Xipeng, commander of the 4th Cavalry Division, Feng Zhian, commander of the 37th Division, Zhang Zizhong, commander of the 38th Division, Dong Yingbin, commander of the 118th Division, Zhang Decheng, commander of the 1st Cavalry Division, Zhu Hongxun, commander of the 130th Division, Huang Guanghua, commander of the 139th Division, and brigade commanders Liang Kai, Li Jintian, and Fu Chun. Together with Yang Zhengzhi, commander of the 108th Division, Zhang Tingshu, commander of the 112th Division, Zhou Fucheng, commander of the 129th Division, and Huang Xiansheng, commander of the 2nd Cavalry Division, who arrived in Hankou on the 11th, there are more than ten people in total. Except for Huang Jie, Feng Zhian, Zhang Zizhong, Huang Guanghua, Li Jintian, and Fu Chun, who took the Jiangxin steamer east at 8:00 PM on the 13th, the rest stayed in Hankou to wait for Zhang. It is said that Zhang is scheduled to summon and train the division and brigade commanders on the 14th. After listening to the training, the division and brigade commanders will take the steamer to Jiangxi that evening. These are all the first batch summoned from the provinces of Hebei and Chahar. As for the second batch summoned to Jiangxi, there are 13 people: Division Commanders Feng Zhanhai, Li Xingcun, Miao Chengliu, Sun Dequan, He Lizhong, Wu Keren, Li Zhentang, Chen Guanqun, Du Jiwu, Bai Fengxiang, Guan Linzheng, Yao Dongfan, and Wang Qifeng. There are nine brigade commanders: Huang Weigang, Xia Ziming, Li Zengzhi, Wang Zhibang, Huang Yongan, Huo Shouyi, Wang Hehua, Zheng Dongguo, and Qiao Fang. They are scheduled to gather in Beiping in late March and concentrate in Nanchang before the 31st. The third batch summoned to Jiangxi includes Division Commanders Zhao Dengyu, Liu Ruming, and Chang Jingwu, and Brigade Commanders Tong Zeguang, Wang Xishan, Liu Zizhen, Gao Pengyun, Luo Qi, and Zhang Yao, totaling six people. They are scheduled to gather in Beiping in early April and concentrate in Nanchang before the 15th of next month. All have decided to visit Zhang when passing through Hankou. The division and brigade commanders from Shaanxi and Shandong have also set off separately. As for the two army commanders, Wang Yizhe and Wan Fulin, and Army Commander He Zhuguo, who are staying in Hankou, they are all planning to stay for a few more days before returning north to their defensive positions. (13th)

Opening of Wuxian Agricultural Products Exhibition

—Location: Zhiyuan in the South of the City—

The day before yesterday (the 12th) was the 9th anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's death and Arbor Day. The Jiangsu Provincial Rice Experiment Field, in conjunction with the Wuxian Agricultural Extension Institute, took advantage of school holidays to hold a three-day agricultural products cooperation exhibition at Zhiyuan in the south of the city. The weather was fine that day, and people from all walks of life flocked to visit the exhibition. At 9:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held in the auditorium. First, the chairman, representing the county magistrate, performed the ceremony. Then, Director Song reported on the opening situation. Next, a representative of the Party Headquarters took the stage to give a speech, with pointed and insightful remarks, criticizing many weaknesses of the current society. Subsequently, trees were planted and photographs were taken in the garden before dispersing. Agricultural and sericultural achievements were displayed in two rooms. Agricultural products mainly consisted of rice and mulberry tree specimens, as well as diagrams and tables of forestry, livestock, and poultry, all displayed in the auditorium. Sericultural achievements mainly consisted of products produced in various villages in the Wuxian district over the years, supplemented by silkworm disease models, microscopes, and various silk products, all displayed in the Panxi Jingshe. Various specimens were hung on all four sides of the corridor, providing a lot for China's agricultural sector to learn from. It is reported that various educational groups will also visit the exhibition in the next two days.

Appeal Dismissed in Medicinal Property Lawsuit

—Shandong High Court Upholds Original Judgment—

Jinan Correspondence: Wang Shilang, a third-generation traditional Chinese medicine practitioner from Qingdao, was involved in a lawsuit because he used ginseng and wulingzhi together to treat postpartum blood disorders in a woman, and the patient died several days later. The Qingdao court ruled that Wang was not proficient in the medicinal properties of herbs, their roles in a prescription, and that his negligence in practice led to the death of the patient. He was sentenced to a fine of 100 yuan. Wang did not accept the ruling and appealed to the Shandong High Court. The court session was held on the 5th of this month, and the debate concluded. The verdict was announced on the 8th, dismissing the appeal. Wang still intends to continue the appeal. The verdict was announced today, and its text is as follows:

"Shandong High Court Criminal Verdict: Appellant Wang Shilang, attorney Zhou Feng (lawyer), the above appellant, in the case of causing death due to negligence in practice, did not accept the first instance judgment of the Qingdao District Court of the Republic of China on January 11, 1934, and filed an appeal. The verdict of this court is as follows:

Main text: The appeal is dismissed.

Facts: Wang Shilang has been practicing medicine for a long time. On August 21, 1933, he treated Ms. Hou Zhang for her illness. Due to his shallow knowledge and lack of attention, he mistakenly used ginseng and wulingzhi, which are incompatible, together, causing Ms. Hou Zhang's illness to worsen. She died on the night of the 26th of the same month. Ms. Hou Liu filed a lawsuit that was investigated and prosecuted by the prosecutor.

Reasons: According to Ms. Hou Liu's statement, her daughter-in-law (Ms. Hou Zhang) fell ill 21 days after giving birth, suffering from headaches. She took the medicine at 11:00 AM. After taking the medicine, she could not speak. She used her hands to grab her stomach. She died at 6:00 PM yesterday (August 26, 1933). Hou Xueyi also stated that Ms. Hou Zhang asked the doctor on August 11 or 12. At 2:00 PM, she could not speak, and her stomach became bloated. She could not pass stool or urine. The doctor said that he could not give her medicine because two of the herbs in the prescription were incompatible, as evidenced by You Xiaoting's statement that the prescription contained wulingzhi and Korean ginseng, and that ginseng and wulingzhi are dangerous together (probably a mistake for the word "wèi" meaning to fear, or to be incompatible), and should not be prescribed together. Ms. Hou Zhang's stomach became bloated, and she could not pass stool or urine or speak after taking the medicine, which was obviously caused by the medicine's effects. The appellant admitted that he prescribed the medicine. Not only did he not describe the illness in the prescription, but he also did not record the pulse. During the investigation and trial, he repeatedly claimed that it was postpartum blood deficiency, postpartum blood blockage, or postpartum blood stasis. When asked if there was an external infection, he replied that there was an external infection. When asked how he knew there was an external infection, he replied that she had a headache because of blood stasis, her body was dry, her pulse was wiry and turbid, and her skin was cold. It is clear that he did not pay attention to the cause of Ms. Hou Zhang's illness. Without identifying the illness, he prescribed ginseng and wulingzhi, which are incompatible, causing her illness to worsen. He was unable to cure her and she died. The original judgment stated that the appellant caused death due to negligence in practice and, according to Article 191, Paragraph 2, and Article 55, Paragraph 3, of the Criminal Code, sentenced him to a fine of 100 yuan, with compulsory execution. If he fails to pay, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day (omitting Article 55, Paragraph 2, of the Criminal Code), which is appropriate. The appellant's arguments are all evasive and cannot be said to be reasonable. Based on the above reasoning, in accordance with Article 384 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text. Prosecutor Li Changfu performed his duties in court in this case. The court of appeal is the Supreme Court, and the appeal deadline is 10 days, starting from the date of delivery of the judgment. March 9, 1934, Presiding Judge Gao Xianzhuo, Judge Wang Shirun, Judge Zhang Kun, Criminal Third Tribunal, Shandong High Court." (March 10)

Songjiang

Preparations for the Third National Products Exhibition

In order to promote the sale of national products and increase public awareness, Shanghai national products manufacturers have consulted and agreed to establish the Third National Products Exhibition in the auditorium of the Songjiang People's Education Hall. Suzhou

Robbery in Lukou Lujiazhuang

Five bandits arrived at Lujiazhuang, Lukou Township, at 2:00 AM on the 13th and wantonly robbed the home of Zhu Dexing, a villager. They severely injured Zhu's wife, Gong, and mother, Cao, on their heads and waists with iron bars. The total loss is estimated to be over 200 yuan.

Raising Funds for the Construction of the Su-Chang Road

The survey and mapping of the Su-Chang Road have been completed, and construction will begin soon. However, 140,000 yuan is needed. After submitting a request to the province for allocation, instructions were received yesterday (the 14th) that the National Economic Commission cannot allocate funds because the road is not listed in the budget. The provincial department also has no funds to subsidize it. In addition to the 70,000 yuan, half the required amount, that has been borrowed by the county, the remaining 70,000 yuan will also be raised by the county government, and construction will begin soon.

Nanhui

Small Boat Collision Injures Ticket Seller

The Xin'an small boat in Xinchang Township travels back and forth between Xinkai and Xiasha and other places four times a day. The boat owner, Ye Zhou, recently found that the boat had few passengers and used more fuel, fearing that it would be difficult to maintain. He rented another Huikang small boat to operate as usual. The original boat was rented to Zhou Xiaodi, who sold tickets on the boat. However, because they were on the same route, disputes often arose, and resentment deepened. At 9:00 AM the day before yesterday, the Huikang boat arrived in Xiasha and was suddenly collided with by the Xin'an boat. Fortunately, no accident occurred. Unexpectedly, at 3:00 PM the same afternoon, after the Huikang boat arrived in Xiasha, the stern was broken by the Xin'an boat's collision. Ye Zhou and the ticket seller A Haosheng went to Zhou Xiaodi to argue, but Zhou Xiaodi used a three-foot-long iron bar to hit the ticket seller into the river, causing serious injuries. After being rescued, he reported to the local security regiment, which took Zhou Xiaodi into custody and transferred him to the county government for interrogation.

Wuxi

Tax Collector Accused of Embezzlement

Xu Jigong, director of the local slaughter tax collection office, has been repeatedly accused by local people, including Hu Chao, to the Provincial Education Fund Management Office of embezzling public funds and engaging in private wrongdoing. Recently, Mao Jinshan, a local resident, stated that the supplementary tax collected in June, July, August, and the first half of September of the 21st year totaled more than 13,000 yuan in the county. However, the director underreported the amount, claiming that slaughterers were in arrears, but in reality, he pocketed the money. Gu Yunpeng, a member sent by the province, also sent a telegram from Yancheng to Wuxi last year, reporting the supplementary tax revenue to the province and county at one-third of the actual amount, openly engaging in fraud and colluding with Lian Shaoshan and others. Therefore, yesterday, he specially submitted a petition to the Provincial Education Fund Management Office, requesting a thorough investigation and strict prosecution.

Strange News of a Sow Giving Birth to an Elephant

Shen, a resident of Xijie Village, Yuqi Township (Qingcheng City), District 15 in the county, had a sow that suddenly gave birth to an elephant at 8:00 AM on the 13th. It was black in color with a long nose, and its head resembled an elephant, while its lower body was that of a pig. It died soon after. Villagers who heard the news went to see it, causing a traffic jam. It was then taken by Chongwen Elementary School in the town, soaked in medicinal water, and displayed in the school for people to visit. It is indeed a strange occurrence.

Changzhou

Street Sweeper Strangled to Death

Old Liu, a street sweeper in Wu Yi Bu Tou Town, for unknown reasons, suddenly died in the night by strangulation. The County Court, upon receiving the report, dispatched Prosecutor Guan Junjie at 8 PM on the 12th to conduct an inquest. He stayed overnight in the town. At approximately 6 AM on the 13th, he arrived at the scene of the death and ordered the coroner to perform an autopsy according to the law. The autopsy revealed that the death was indeed caused by strangulation. If it were a suicide by hanging, there would not have been rope marks all around the neck, and fresh blood would not have been vomited from the mouth. Prosecutor Guan, considering the case involved human life, began an investigation in the town and discovered that the case involved an affair. He ordered the police to summon five individuals involved: Ma San, Yi Gongliang, Qu Zhongbao, Chen Daguanzi, and Fu Shusheng. Ma San’s daughter, who was allegedly intimate with Old Liu, had fled. After interrogation, he ordered that all be taken to the city for further investigation and prosecution.

Nantong

Court Orders Exhumation for Revenge Killing Inquest

Huang Shengkang, a detective from Shanghai, who lived in Chuan Gang, was suddenly assassinated by an enemy last month upon returning to Tong. His family reported to the court, but without waiting for the prosecutor to arrive for an inquest, they proceeded with the encoffining. Chief Prosecutor Liu has now sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau to seal and transport the coffin to the city for exhumation and inquest.

Qingjiang

Two Kidnapping Cases Outside the City

The residents inside and outside Huaiyin City are somewhat panicked due to the change of guard between the stationed army and the Provincial Security Team. However, the area outside the city is vast, making it difficult for the military and police to provide adequate protection. Yesterday (the 10th) after 6 PM, several bandits went to the home of Zhang Wenyuan in Tangzi Alley, north of the city. They first brandished handguns to intimidate Zhang’s family and prevent them from making noise, then abducted Zhang Wenyuan from the back door. This was discovered by Ding, the company commander of the mountain artillery unit of the Provincial Security Team stationed nearby, who immediately led his troops in pursuit. Zhang was shot and dropped by the bandits outside Beiwei, and had already been wounded by gunfire. At the same time, bandits also went to the Zhao Hengxing lumberyard at Yangqiaokou and kidnapped Zhao Huanzhi’s young daughter. By the time the military and police arrived to pursue and suppress them, the bandits had disappeared.

Funing

Police Team Recovers Kidnapping Victim

Hu Zhushou Peng, of the police squad stationed in Gou Dun Town, received a report yesterday that bandits were hiding a kidnapping victim in Tianjia She. He immediately dispatched a team to investigate and recovered one victim, while the bandits had already fled. It is reported that the victim is Yuan Guangqian’s son, who was kidnapped by bandits last winter. The team has already presented the victim to the brigade headquarters, awaiting identification by his family.

International Commercial Telegram

—Reuters Special Commercial Report, March 14th—

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today (14th), the London gold price is 136 shillings and 1 penny, down 1 1/2 pence from yesterday’s price.

London Silver: Today's silver market remained unchanged. Spot price is 20 pence 625, and futures price is 20 pence 75. India bought and China sold in the morning. The market closed peacefully.

New York Silver: Today (14th), the New York silver market did not attract much attention. The market was sluggish, and operators adopted a cautious attitude due to the lack of new developments and the silence of the government regarding the silver proposal. Today's closing price rose by 10 to 15 points compared to yesterday's closing price.

Bombay Silver: Today (14th), the Bombay silver market closed quietly. The spot price fell by 2 annas to 56 rupees and 8 annas. All futures fell by 4 annas.

Exchange Rates

British-American Exchange Rate: This morning (14th), the London exchange market was more stable. The British-American exchange rate opened at $5.09875, compared to yesterday's US/UK angle of 0.0625, and one US dollar was equivalent to 3 shillings and 11 pence 0012.

British-French Exchange Rate: The London market opened at 77 francs 43 against the French exchange rate, falling 3 points, then rose to 77 francs 59, then fell back to 77 francs 53, which was 10 points higher than the opening price.

US-UK Exchange Rate: The New York exchange rate against the British exchange rate closed at 5.09875 on the previous day, opened at 75 today, 2nd trade 75, 3rd trade 625, 4th trade 50, 5th trade 50.

US-French Exchange Rate: The New York exchange rate against the French exchange rate opened at 6.5825.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The cotton market is still eagerly awaiting the development of the Bankhead Act. It opened quietly today (14th) with minimal fluctuations. Local, Southern, and Japanese merchants sold slightly, but it was absorbed by purchases from peers and Wall Street. The market situation was unremarkable in the morning.

Bombay Cotton: Today (14th), the Bombay cotton market was stable despite speculative selling, as Japanese merchants had a strong demand for spot goods. At closing, the price of April-May white rose cotton was 201 rupees, up 75.

Liverpool Cotton: Yesterday's cotton market's firmness could not be maintained today (14th). At 1 PM, the price for May futures was 6.27, down 5 points.

Liverpool Wheat: Today (14th), the wheat market was relatively loose. The May futures price was 4 shillings 3 pence 75, down 25 from yesterday.

However, merchants are still cautious. Before long, the market situation turned sluggish, but confidence remained stable, and the increase at the opening could still be maintained. Local News

Sun Fo Flew to Nanchang Yesterday

Kong to stay for one or two days before returning to Beijing via Shanghai.

To discuss central financial matters with Chiang.

Sun Fo, President of the Legislative Yuan, and Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance, upon invitation from Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, jointly flew to Jiangxi yesterday morning aboard a Ford aircraft. They will discuss important issues such as central finance and the reorganization of southwestern politics. A reporter from the New News Agency learned from the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance that Kong sent a telegram to Shanghai immediately after flying to Jiangxi from Beijing, stating, "We arrived safely in Nanchang at 1 PM today (the 14th). We plan to stay in Jiangxi for one or two days before returning to Beijing via Shanghai."

Song Ziwen Went to Beijing Yesterday

Visited Dai Jitao again yesterday morning.

Departed at the beginning of the month to inspect the Northwest.

Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council, in order to finalize the development plans for the Northwest, decided to go to the Northwest with Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan, for an on-the-spot inspection. Song and Dai had met once in Shanghai to discuss everything. Song visited Dai’s residence on Avenue Haig at about 10 AM yesterday morning for further discussions, and left after an hour. It is reported that it has been largely decided that they will depart at the beginning of next month. The inspection location will be centered on Shaanxi. Other places such as Gansu and Qinghai can only be determined after arriving in Shaanxi due to transportation and war conditions. Song took the night train to Beijing last night to ask the central government for instructions. After returning to Shanghai and making some preparations, he can set off.

Temporary Alert Yesterday

Strict precautions at the border between the Chinese and foreign concessions.

Dagong News Agency reports that yesterday was the anniversary of the establishment of the Soviet government by the Communists. The police authorities of the Chinese and foreign concessions in the city, fearing that the Communist elements would take the opportunity to disrupt public order during this time of thriving labor unrest, specially announced a temporary alert for one day. At major roads along the Chinese and foreign concession borders in the southern city, double posts were added. Inspectors and detectives, along with plainclothes inspectors, conducted strict inspections of suspicious pedestrians in the Ximen area. Precautions were especially strict in the Caojiadu area in western Shanghai. The French Concession authorities paid even more attention to preventing disturbances in various places due to the Mei Ya factory strike. All detectives were stationed in areas bordering the Chinese and foreign concessions to maintain peace within the concession.

Fujian Party Affairs Instructor

Chen Zhaoying Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Scheduled to take a ship to Fujian on the 17th to take office.

The design committee has been finalized and will be announced today.

Central News Agency reports that Chen Zhaoying, the special envoy of the central government to serve as the Fujian Party Affairs Instructor, arrived in Beijing from his native place in the Pujiang area a few days ago to ask the central government for instructions. He completed his official business at 11 PM the night before last and took a night train to Shanghai with his entourage, Zhao Weimin. He arrived at the North Station at 7:30 AM yesterday morning and went to his hotel to rest. Chen is scheduled to take the Jardine Matheson & Co. Chefoo to Fujian on the 17th to take office. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Chen at his hotel yesterday and was given the following statement:

Steps to Reorganize Party Affairs in Fujian Province

According to Chen, party affairs in Fujian Province have been completely suspended since the outbreak of the Fujian Rebellion. After arriving, he will first meet with the Fujian Province Party Affairs Design Committee to start organizing lower-level party branches. Once the party organization is sound, he will convene a provincial representative assembly to elect members to the provincial party headquarters and supervisory committee, and establish a formal party headquarters. The task of himself and the Fujian Province Party Affairs Design Committee will end after the provincial party headquarters is established.

Design Committee Members to Be Announced Today

The number of members of the Fujian Province Party Affairs Design Committee is seven, with an additional secretary-general. The candidates have already been internally decided: Zheng Zuyin, Chen Meian, Fang Zhongzheng, Tang Deming, Zhu Wanlin, Zhan Xiaohuan, and Xie Dongshan as committee members, and Zhao Weimin as secretary-general. Today (the 15th), the list will be submitted to the Central Standing Committee for approval and formal announcement.

Contacting Military and Government Officials to Jointly Plan Construction

In the past, party affairs in Fujian did not have special achievements. In the future, he will encourage party comrades to unite sincerely, break down regional prejudices, and make the party, government, and military work together towards construction. Fujian was originally a wealthy place, but years of chaos and heavy taxes have caused resources to be abandoned underground, and no one dares to develop them. In the future, efforts must be made to stabilize society so that overseas Chinese can invest in Fujian with peace of mind and develop resources. In ten years, Fujian will be wealthy and the party can be the best in the country.

Mr. Hu Zhantang Will Not Leave Hong Kong Temporarily

Finally, the reporter asked whether recent rumors that Mr. Hu Zhantang was about to go to Beijing were true. Chen said that during this time of serious national crisis, Mr. Hu Zhantang will go to Beijing sooner or later to share the burden, but he has not heard of the rumors that Mr. Hu is "about" to go to Beijing, and it is probably too early to say so. Although he has not had contact with Mr. Hu recently, Mr. Hu is probably still living in Hong Kong and will not go to Beijing immediately.

Cotton Mills to Reduce Working Hours

Decision made to implement starting in June.

Methods to be decided at another meeting.

The cotton spinning industry has been declining in recent years. Since last year, cotton mills have been reducing working hours or suspending operations from time to time. The phenomenon of cheap yarn and expensive cotton has not been resolved, and the industry is in increasingly dire straits. Stagnant yarn sales are especially painful for businesses. Various Chinese-owned yarn mills in this city and other ports, seeing this situation, must quickly seek unanimous relief, otherwise they will be plunged into a desperate situation. A discussion meeting was convened yesterday afternoon to discuss both palliative and fundamental solutions. More than 40 mills attended, with Rong Zongjing as chairman. The following methods were decided: (1) Starting this month, if the yarn produced by each mill is directly or indirectly delivered to the exchange, the mill will be responsible for taking it back in the month following the delivery. The penalties for violating this resolution will be discussed and decided at another meeting next Wednesday. (2) Starting on June 1, each mill will reduce working hours to reduce production. The methods will be decided at another meeting. There are currently 58 yarn mills in this city and other ports, with approximately 1.1 million spindles. It has been decided to implement the reduction in working hours starting on June 1.

Special District

Rickshaw Owners Held a General Meeting Yesterday

Establishment of a design committee to plan rickshaw pullers' relief.

Send representatives to negotiate with the Public Works Department to improve harsh penalties.

Central News Agency reports that after the Public Works Department's Human-Powered Vehicle Committee suggested to the Public Works Department that it should take back 2,000 public rickshaws in the Special District, reduce rental prices, provide relief to rickshaw pullers, and establish a new company to change the way licenses are issued, the Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association's Special District Office believed that this measure would have a significant impact on the industry's operations and the livelihood of rickshaw owners. Therefore, it held a general meeting of all operators in the Special District at 10 AM yesterday at the city's Chamber of Commerce auditorium to discuss countermeasures. The meeting adjourned at about 1 PM. The details are as follows:

Meeting Proceedings

Yesterday, 813 rickshaw operators and owners attended the meeting. Zhang Huaiyang, representative of the Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association, and Chen Guoliang, representative of the rickshaw pullers' union, attended as observers. After the meeting was called to order, Yin Zhiling, Liang Ruiting, Gu Songmao, Zheng Jiansan, and Liu Zhenqiu were elected as the presidium of the meeting. After the formalities, Presidium Member Gu Songmao reported the purpose of the meeting, Yin Zhiling reported on the negotiations with the Public Works Department authorities, and Liu Zhenqiu read the general assembly's declaration, which was unanimously approved. The discussion of the motions then began. The atmosphere at the meeting was tense, and it adjourned at 1 PM.

Motions Passed

(1) The motion of the board of directors drafting a declaration for the general assembly to vote on was passed. (2) The motion of Chen Guoliang, representative of the rickshaw pullers' union, requesting to attend as an observer and bringing the union's official letter proposing the adoption of opinions on rickshaw pullers' relief was approved. The proposed opinions were handed over to the board of directors for review. (3) The motion on how to plan and proceed with rickshaw pullers' relief was approved. A design committee was established. In addition to all directors serving as committee members, Zheng Jiansan, Cai Shengnan, and Mao Guangcai were appointed as design committee members. (4) The motion to plan for the construction costs of a new village was approved. It was tentatively set at five yuan per rickshaw. (5) The motion to standardize the rental prices for rickshaws among operators was approved. The board of directors will consider the situation of rickshaw owners, renters, and pullers within one month, set the prices, and then notify them for implementation. (6) The motion to request permission for the rickshaw industry to send several representatives to attend the Public Works Department's vehicle affairs meeting and the Public Works Department's traffic committee meeting at 4 PM today was approved. Gu Songmao and Yin Zhiling were appointed to attend today's Public Works Department Traffic Committee and subsequent vehicle affairs meetings. (7) The motion regarding the harsh vehicle inspections and long detention periods of licenses by the Public Works Department recently, and the need for negotiations. (8) The motion regarding rickshaw pullers being insulted by Public Works Department constables and the need to provide relief from unwarranted penalties for violations. It was decided that Yin and Gu would be responsible for the above two motions.

Sending Representatives to Negotiate

In addition to appointing Yin Zhiling and Gu Songmao to go to the Public Works Department's Traffic Committee for negotiations at 4 PM yesterday, the association also prepared a petition and submitted it to the Public Works Department. The document stated, "To the Public Works Department, the rickshaw owners held a general meeting of all operators at the city's Chamber of Commerce auditorium on the 14th of this month. They had extensive discussions on improving rickshaws, providing relief to rickshaw pullers, and appropriately reducing and standardizing rental prices. In addition to issuing a declaration, there are also (1)

Recently, the Public Works Department's vehicle inspection office has been excessively harsh, detaining licenses for as long as one day or three days to two weeks for any defects in the vehicles. This not only forces rickshaw owners to suspend operations but also deprives rickshaw pullers of their livelihoods. Please allow fines to be imposed on the spot to avoid losses for both rickshaw owners and pullers. (2) When rickshaw pullers are operating, they are often insulted by constables on false pretenses and subjected to harsh penalties, such as license detention. Since rickshaw owners must improve and provide relief, the authorities should also make necessary corrections. The above situations must be improved. The relevant cases have been recorded and a letter is attached, along with the declaration, for your review. We respectfully request that you adopt and implement these measures, which would be in the public interest." All of this was unanimously approved on file.

Declaration of the General Assembly

The awarding of merits and the punishment of demerits are inherently within the purview of the authorities' governance, and any changes in policy should be based on reasonable and justifiable measures. Recently, upon reviewing the report of the Shanghai Municipal Council (SMC) Public Ricksha Committee published in the SMC Gazette Special Edition of February 23rd of this year, we find that the contributions of the Public Ricksha Industry Association of the Special District have been entirely disregarded. Instead, the Committee relies on incomplete and inaccurate investigations, or even manipulative statements and fabricated accusations, as the basis for its report. Consequently, the Committee recklessly speculates that existing ricksha owners lack any sincerity in improving their vehicles or assisting ricksha pullers. It even proposes to revoke two thousand of the currently licensed rickshas annually from January 1, 1935, and transfer them to a new company whose organization and all conditions are to be approved and controlled by the SMC. We ask, is this kind of proposal in accordance with legal principles or even human sentiment? Ricksha owners unanimously and resolutely oppose this proposal. Their reasons for opposition, in addition to the Special District Office having already pointed out the inaccuracies in the Committee's report regarding the total number of rickshas, total license fees, costs and expenses, net profits of ricksha owners, and the extreme deterioration of vehicles, and submitting these points to the SMC authorities, are as follows: (1) The report proposes that the organization of the new company should be controlled by the SMC, which is incomprehensible. Since ricksha owners obtained their licenses, they have been operating in accordance with the regulations, with every action and every matter under the strict control of the SMC. Has the Public Ricksha Committee failed to hear of this? (2) The Special District Office has dispatched four cleaning inspectors to inspect the streets daily. When substandard rickshas are found, they are required to be repaired and cleaned. Moreover, tea is provided in the summer, rice in the winter, and three branch and main epidemic hospitals have been established. These improvements to rickshas and assistance to ricksha pullers are all initiated by the ricksha owners themselves. If the SMC wishes to promote and expand these efforts, it should provide clear instructions. If, after repeated orders and appeals, the ricksha owners are unable to accept them within a feasible range, it would not be too late to transfer the business. However, the current vague proposition clearly demonstrates prejudice. (3) According to Article 21 of the SMC License Regulations, licenses may be revoked or temporarily suspended for violations of the regulations. Based on this, there must be a violation of the regulations before there is a risk of license revocation. If punishment is unjustly inflicted, how can the ricksha owners willingly accept it? (4) Even in the event of occasional violations of the regulations, the license revocation must be determined by court judgment. It is noted that, within the industry, ten licenses have been revoked twice, and despite requests from various parties, the authorities have consistently refused to issue new licenses to others. The report's suggestion that the SMC suspend two thousand licenses after December 31, 1934, and allow others to apply for a license to operate is inconsistent with established regulations. (5) At the request of one or two Westerners, regardless of their involvement in the ricksha industry, the Public Ricksha Committee proposes to deprive all ricksha owners, numbering in the thousands, of their legal right to operate a livelihood. If implemented, this would not only harm the ricksha industry, but also set a precedent that could affect all licensed businesses operated by Chinese merchants in the Settlement, causing everyone to feel threatened. (6) It is particularly important to solemnly declare that the Public Ricksha Committee believes that there is a fact of buying and selling rickshas or license plates, and points out that the price of a ricksha ranges from over one hundred yuan to seven hundred and fifty yuan, and the price of a license plate is six hundred and fifty yuan. Although this issue was raised as a question by the representative of the Special District Office in a document submitted to the SMC, if it is not clarified, it may become a matter of suspicion. Public rickshas are operated by independent owners, leased operators, or those who represent or entrust others. There has never been any buying and selling of rickshas. Moreover, license plates are issued by the SMC for operation and are subject to strict regulations, unlike private property that can be freely disposed of. It would be foolish for ricksha owners to create trouble for themselves in this way. In short, things cry out when they are treated unfairly. Since ricksha owners have been operating public rickshas, all losses incurred from the previous changes in ricksha design and wheel modifications have been set aside for the time being. Beginning in 1924, the number of rickshas was first increased and then reduced, resulting in a one-third reduction in the number of qualified rickshas and a one-third increase in the cost of building a ricksha. During the 1928 Northern Expedition and the 1932 Shanghai Incident, traffic was sometimes cut off, and special curfews were imposed, lasting for several months. The ricksha business plummeted. These circumstances are known to all. In addition, in recent years, buses and trams have covered all the roads, and our public rickshas are frequently stopped, which has become commonplace. Moreover, from April to September each year, ricksha pullers return to their hometowns to farm, and most rickshas are idle, which goes without saying. However, the Public Ricksha Committee disregards the various hardships and direct and indirect expenses of ricksha owners. Instead, it only listens to false accusations and exaggerations, and proposes to transfer the business of the majority of people to a new company. Ricksha owners cannot help but urgently and loudly point out the errors in the report and list their reasons for opposition for the world to see. We earnestly request that all sectors of society, based on fairness and justice, make reasonable and appropriate comments and provide assistance so that the hard-earned money of ricksha owners can be spared from unnecessary and significant losses. This should be extended to all licensed businesses, so that they are not similarly affected. However, many ricksha owners have vehicles and licenses that they have acquired through hard work and are well aware of the pains and hardships of ricksha pullers. Now, at the time of the general assembly of all ricksha owners, we will jointly discuss improving ricksha designs to make them easier for ricksha pullers to pull, and the methods of assisting ricksha pullers to improve their lives. We hereby formulate the following articles: A. The Special District Office will send representatives to request the SMC to reissue ten vacant licenses before July of this year to manufacture a standard public ricksha as a model for testing and improving vehicles. B. From January 1, 1935, public rickshas will be gradually improved in accordance with the approved test rickshas. C. A public ricksha pullers' hospital will be established in a central location in the city, with wards capable of accommodating 200 people, as well as complete Chinese and Western medicine and equipment. It is resolved that construction will commence on April 1, 1934, and be completed by January 1, 1935. D. Starting on the same date as item C, four new public ricksha pullers' villages will be constructed, located in the east, south, west, and north of Shanghai. The completion date will be the same as item C. In addition, four new ricksha pullers' villages will be built annually, completing 20 new public ricksha pullers' villages by December 31, 1939, capable of accommodating 20,000 ricksha pullers. E. A Ricksha Pullers' Hospital and New Village Construction Committee will be established, with representatives selected by the Special District Office and representatives from the three local authorities of this city invited to participate for supervision. The construction costs will be borne on average by the ricksha owners of the Special District, and the municipal authorities and charitable organizations will be requested to provide assistance. F. Each ricksha pullers' village must have at least 1,000 dormitory rooms for ricksha pullers, as well as public bathrooms, cooperative dining halls, classrooms, and assembly halls to facilitate ricksha pullers' education and hygiene. G. Ricksha pullers residing in the new villages may directly solicit business from various ricksha companies. The rental portion of their rickshas will be reduced appropriately. (1) The amount will be set to ensure uniformity. (2) The lessee receives one-quarter of the rental price to maintain their livelihood and is not allowed to demand additional payments. In short, the rental price should be in line with the situation so that all parties do not feel unfairly treated. In addition to submitting the above measures to the authorities for review and approval, and requesting that two representatives be sent to participate in meetings so that ricksha owners can effectively improve rickshas and provide assistance to maintain the ricksha industry, this declaration is hereby made for your consideration.

Page 12

Shanghai Banking Syndicate 6% Securities

Scheduled for Issuance on April 15th

Designated Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Principal and Interest as the Fund

Principal Repaid Every Six Months, Cleared in Six Years

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Ministry of Finance borrowed 44 million yuan from Shanghai banks, with the Italian return of Boxer Indemnity funds as the repayment fund. The borrowing banks formed the Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Syndicate and issued the 6% Securities of the 1934 Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Syndicate. These are now in print and scheduled for issuance on the 15th of next month. Details are as follows:

Tranches to be Disbursed to the Ministry

The Ministry of Finance borrowed 44 million yuan from Shanghai banks, divided into 4,400 shares of 10,000 yuan each. The Central Bank accounted for 6.71 million yuan, the Bank of China for 8.8 million yuan, the Bank of Communications for 4.4 million yuan, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank for 3.52 million yuan, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank for 3.52 million yuan, the Zhejiang Xingye Bank for 1.65 million yuan, the China & South Sea Bank for 2.2 million yuan, the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank for 2.2 million yuan, the Jin Cheng Banking Corporation for 2.2 million yuan, the Continental Bank for 2.2 million yuan, the National Industrial Bank of China for 2.2 million yuan, the China United Industrial Bank for 1.1 million yuan, the National Commercial Bank for 1.1 million yuan, the Kending Bank for 1.1 million yuan, the Tung Lai Bank for 550,000 yuan, and the Bank of Jiangsu for 550,000 yuan. Among them, the Bank of China has the most, followed by the Central Bank and then the Bank of Communications. It is stipulated that the funds will be delivered to the Ministry of Finance in four equal monthly installments.

Scheduled Issuance

The Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Syndicate Office, jointly established by sixteen banks including the Central Bank, has moved to the upstairs of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank building on Jiangxi Road and is issuing 30 million yuan of 6% Securities of the 1934 Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Syndicate in accordance with Article 11 of the loan contract signed with the Ministry of Finance, "Before this loan is fully repaid, the syndicate may use the remaining balance of this loan as a fund for issuing bonds. The issuance method shall be determined by the syndicate itself." The securities are now in print and scheduled for issuance on April 15th.

Approved by the Ministry of Finance

The Syndicate submitted an application to the Ministry of Finance for approval and filing for the issuance of securities. Excerpts of the provisions are as follows: (1) Name: 6% Securities of the 1934 Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Syndicate; (2) Quota: 30 million yuan in national currency; (3) Issuance Date: April 15, 1934; (4) Interest Rate: 6% per annum, with interest paid every six months; (5) Principal Repayment: Principal will be repaid every six months by lottery; (6) Term: Repaid in twelve installments over six years from the date of issuance; (7) Institutions Paying Principal and Interest: Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications; (8) Fund: This syndicate will designate the principal and interest fund payable by the Ministry of Finance under the Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan contract as the fund, and this syndicate shall be fully responsible for repayment; (9) Issuance Price: Issued at par; (10) Types of Securities: 10,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan denominations; (11) Repurchase Price: This syndicate may repurchase the securities upon three months' notice. If the market price of the securities is higher than the face value on the date of the notice, they will be repurchased according to the market price on the date of the notice. If the market price is lower than the face value, they will be repurchased at par. All interest will be calculated on a daily basis at the face value from the date of the notice until the date of repurchase.

Temporary Suspension

The New Voice reporter learned from banking circles in Shanghai yesterday that 4.4 million yuan of the Ministry of Finance's loan of 44 million yuan, one-eleventh of the total, will be retained by the syndicate to temporarily pay the interest due on the loan if the surplus of customs revenue is insufficient to pay the interest. The disbursement of funds by each bank will be without any deductions. The syndicate will issue the securities at par. The loan interest rate is 8% per month, and the securities interest rate is 6% per week. The loan term is 15 years, and the securities term is 6 years. The syndicate, which has undertaken the loan, has scheduled to disburse the funds to the Ministry of Finance within four months from the 1st of this month, but the issuance of securities by the syndicate has recently been temporarily suspended due to a certain issue, so it is still uncertain whether the issuance will be approved on April 15th.
