Reading Room Answers

A Discussion of Reading Methodology (4)

The editor has discussed the general issues of reading methodology based on the questions raised by Mr. Wang's letter. Now, I will discuss some experiences in reading techniques with Mr. Wang. - Editor

The first priority in reading is, of course, to emphasize methodology. With a methodology, one's thinking will not be scattered, and one can gain systematic knowledge. However, when reading a book, how can one ensure that reading the book is not the same as not reading it? How can one gain inspiration from the book? How can one remember the important content of the book, or a few brilliant sentences of the author, and what one considers to be wrong? Or what method can be used to facilitate future review? This kind of "reading efficiency" method should also be emphasized. We said earlier that when reading casually, after reading a book, the content of the book may be remembered at the time, but this vague impression will be quickly forgotten after a while. Moreover, when reading introductory books such as "Introduction" or "Outline" of a certain subject, the outline and basic principles of this kind of book should be fully memorized in one's heart. It is useless to remember the meaning of a certain principle in a fragmented way, even if it is remembered in great detail. This kind of book should have its important content evenly memorized, but there is no need to memorize any particular part of it. Now, I will provide a few of the most popular reading methods for your reference.

(1) Underlining - While reading, use red and blue pencils to underline the outline or important sentences in the book. The best place to draw lines for those who usually read Western books is the underline, followed by circles, and then the vertical line next to the page. (2) Marginal Notes - Use one or two sentences or a dozen words to write the main idea of a chapter or section simply on the upper end of the book or on the blank space on both sides of the book. This method is called marginal notes.

(3) Notes - This is the most commonly used method by scholars. It is a very efficient method, but it is also a very clumsy method, because taking notes takes a lot of time. However, if this method is used properly, it is not a loss, so it is still beneficial for busy people like us to read. Notes can be divided into three types: (1) Excerpts - The method is to copy down the author's special views and insightful sentences while reading; (2) Postscript - That is, not only excerpts of sentences, but also criticisms and opinions of the author are written on it; (3) Summary - This method is similar in nature to marginal notes, but there are also completely different points. That is, marginal notes are made as you read, while this is done after reading; marginal notes are written on the original book, while this is written in another notebook; marginal notes are extracted according to the original chapters and sections, while this can establish its own outline at will without being constrained by the original form, and can add opinions. These three methods are all useful, but it depends on your level of reading and the reading material. For example, if you are studying social sciences, and if you have basic knowledge and are reading specialized works or certain issues, then you should use the first method, because specialized issues often have one or two introductory chapters, such as a book discussing the purchasing power of currency, which first describes the nature of currency, various explanations about currency, etc. If you have read a good introduction to economics, you will know all of these things, so you don't need to use marginal notes, underlining, and other methods to take out these things. However, you should pay attention to the author's special opinions on currency, and you should copy these places down. If you are reading the works of famous scholars, then the postscript method is more appropriate, because you can not only copy down its famous sayings, but also write down the criticisms of later generations and your own opinions. But if you do not have basic knowledge, or if you do not have any knowledge of a certain subject, and you are just thinking about doing preliminary research, then you cannot use the first two methods. Because when you enter the subject, you must first read a book of the "Introduction" type of the subject, and most of these books are of the nature of textbooks, so what they describe is the most popular theory, which is the general nature of the subject. There are no particularly brilliant chapters and sentences in these books for you to extract, but the important principles or outlines of the subject, you should remember, so using the summary method, or the combination of summary and marginal notes, is better.

In short, taking notes is for the secondary purpose of preparing for future reading, the most important thing is that taking notes allows you to circulate the things described in the book in your brain for a while, so that you can consider what the author said. Therefore, the first method is the least economical among these three methods. We waste a lot of energy on doing this kind of work, so this method is very useful for writers (because it is convenient to cite when writing), but it is not worth the loss for people like us who do not want to be scholars and writers and who read for practical benefits. However, although this method of extraction is clumsy, the benefits are still there, so we can still use it if we slightly modify its method. The reason why this method is clumsy is that it has to be copied sentence by sentence, which is really too time-consuming, but if we do not copy it sentence by sentence, and use simple sentences to summarize the original meaning by ourselves, and at the same time write down the book title, person's name, volume and page number, so as to facilitate future reading, in this way, the time spent is not much, and the benefits are not reduced.

(4) Rereading - Some people like to read a lot of books, but are unwilling to read a good book carefully or read it several times. This is a big problem. Why is this kind of reading wrong? The reason is this: When readers read a book for the first time, they are actually "clueless", thinking that knowledge is "as vast as the sea", and books are "piling up like cows". Indeed, this is true. But he therefore wants to read all kinds of books as much as possible, which is a big problem. There are dozens of introductory books on a subject in the market. Some people think that they should all be read once, but this is actually a big mistake. The content of these books is roughly the same. You only need to choose a more carefully reviewed book and read it several times, and remember the content, which is better than reading all kinds of books indiscriminately. As a result, you will get confused, and you will know nothing about the general nature of the subject. The pros and cons are really incalculable. Therefore, reading good books several times will not only not waste time, but is very economical. Because when you read a book for the first time, the impression must be very shallow. When you read it again, you will definitely discover many places that you neglected last time, and you can also understand the author's opinions more deeply. But this of course refers to authoritative works, or books that should be read carefully. Of course, there is no need to put in this kind of effort for a class of books that are only suitable for browsing. The method of reading is roughly the same, but you should not stick to the rules, and you should try and modify it at any time. Also, the methods described in this article, except for a slight supplement by the editor based on personal experience, are mostly described by Yuhiko Tsurumi's "The Method of Reading". See Thoughts, Landscapes, People, page 121. Published by Beixin.) If you have time, you may wish to read that article.

Spring and Autumn

Prepare! Our Skills!

— A Call to Arms

The 10th Far Eastern Games will soon open in the Philippines!

The 2nd World Games are scheduled to open in Berlin in 1936! One is close at hand; the other seems still far away.

For the Far Eastern Games close at hand, our attendance and selection issues are being discussed by the Chinese National Sports Association. For the Summer Olympics far away, the general public does not seem to have paid attention yet.

According to recent telegrams: More than 50 countries have received letters from Germany inviting them to participate in the Summer Olympics to be held in Berlin in 1936. In the invitation letter, the Germanic nation stated its hope that friendly countries around the world would generously agree to participate and send elite athletes to compete in friendly sportsmanship.

German Chancellor Hitler has decided to designate a 285-acre open space in the Spreefelsburg district of western Berlin, with lush forests, as the venue for the Games. Construction is underway for a stadium that can accommodate 100,000 spectators; outside the stadium, an entertainment area that can accommodate 250,000 people will be set up.

The German Sports Association's special meeting has already decided: "Each village and city across the country will hold competitive competitions to select athletes; then, athletes from various regions will gather to compete, carefully select talent, and give them long-term special training. The government will provide full support!"

On the world stage, we have almost never had a role! We haven't even grasped the tail of all the techniques! With the same skills, why can't we compete with others?

In the 1932 Summer Olympics held in Los Angeles, among the 45 countries that participated, India also scored five points. Tiny Switzerland and Uruguay also scored four or five points each. Our "neighbor"—Japan—after all, had face, scoring 153 points to get the sixth place in the entire Games. At that time, our representative was only Liu Changchun. Our score was a big goose egg!

For the 1936 Summer Olympics, are we going to Berlin to touch goose eggs again? Even touching goose eggs requires preparing several qualified skills. Otherwise, we won't even have the chance to touch goose eggs; that would be even more unacceptable.

We must prepare the skills to seize the "throne" in the Far East!

We must prepare the skills to touch "goose eggs" in Berlin in 1936!

We must gradually reveal our role on the world stage; because

We possess the same skills!

Spring is Here

— Rong Yu

Spring is here! When people hear the word "spring," they will feel that it contains various meanings of "beauty," "happiness," "vitality," and "renewal." It is not necessary for the various presentations of "spring breeze and peach plum," "spring river and flower moon," and "spring colors are annoying" to know the power of the "god of spring."

"The cat is calling, the dog is jumping" this is the spring thoughts of animals. "A girl is in spring, a gentleman tempts her" This is the spring mood of young masters and young ladies. "A moment in the spring night is worth a thousand gold," that is the cherishing of spring by those who go to dance halls and play with prostitutes. "Spring colors are annoying and sleepless," this is the injury of spring caused by unrequited love. There are really many patterns and all kinds of happiness that can't be said about "spring." I welcome you to come, and I hope you will stay in the world forever, so that everyone is full of spring breeze, full of spring, and permanently preserve the spring gland, and will not die even when they are old.

People in the past couldn't think it through after all, and easily abandoned this great spring, burying themselves in books that "cannot be eaten when hungry and cannot be worn as clothing." The antique Shao Yaofu even said something like "the plan of a year lies in spring," stubbornly dragging many people into the cold palace, which is really not right. It was the wine-loving Li Bai who thought it through, so he said, "The ancients used candles to travel at night, there is a good reason for it." With this argument, he could "day and night" desperately drink alcohol.

In bustling cities, it is spring all the time. Shanghai, known as the Paris of the East, is of course no exception. Once evening comes, the light of the red lights and the singing of the entertainers can be seen and heard everywhere. Sexually suggestive and half-naked movies, and dance halls of fleshy temptation, are all fully booked. The fragrance of wine, the smell of cigarettes, the breath of women, and the light of foreign money fill the night in Shanghai. Shanghai has become a city where it is spring all the time, and men and women are stumbling and falling in this artificially created spring breeze.

Hey! Spring is here! In Shanghai, some young men and women have come to the parks; some people who break peach blossoms by car have increased on Longhua Road; and some high-priced spring fabrics have been sold in foreign companies. Shanghainese only have these amazing achievements regarding spring.

Bulletin Board

— Shi Jihong

The Spring and Autumn Annals has discussed many things; however, regarding schools, I'm afraid it doesn't amount to even a tenth of what has been accumulated since the existence of the Spring and Autumn Annals. Here, I'll add a piece on "bulletin boards" to fill the void!

Putting out a bulletin board is not an easy task, even though it doesn't grandly state who the editor is or who the publisher is. However, if it's not a student with considerable influence in the school, this bulletin board, once pasted on the wall, can be "snowflakes flying" in less than an hour. Even if a glass frame is used, it will be shattered by someone. Otherwise, the school authorities won't approve its establishment. Even if a privately published one is discovered, the bulletin board will be confiscated, and the person will be punished. (Demerits or a grand dressing down also.)

In the literary world, there are mutual attacks. Of course, everyone clashes with their pens. In their respective territories, they don't hesitate to use ample space for personal revenge. In a small way, a bulletin board is no different. For example, the author's school has a certain drama club that was originally scheduled to hold its debut performance on December 24th last year. Hundreds of tickets had already been issued, but due to the relentless attacks of the bulletin board, a fifty-cent ticket is still in the author's pocket today. Alas, the bulletin board. On this small bulletin board, one can obtain many unexpected gains. Although it has no advertisements, subduing younger students for use during general student assemblies, conquering female students so they dare not treat him—the editor—disrespectfully, are all its functions.

As for the manuscripts, of course, there's fundamentally no question. We'll leave aside the discussion of their origins for now. But why does everyone see it as a remedy? Why is the side dish in the dining hall particularly rich? What disputes do the two factions have? As long as he's there, he can settle disputes with a few words. Why are the female students willing to write articles, knit scarves, and make gloves for them unconditionally? The readers are left to ponder.

Five-Colored Poems

— Chen Xiaocui

Red Mourns Lost Territory

Beacon smoke and chaotic fire crows fill the desolate border. Banners and flags cover the land, still Chinese. Dreams awaken in Qin towers to the third pole of the sun. Zhao walls' soldiers shift with the night's bugle. Wronged is your rouge, sharing the shame of the well. Annoying is the color, like cherry blossoms. The setting sun is exactly like a hero's blood, smeared on the city wall as evening haze.

Yellow Worries About Neighboring Bandits

The setting sun falls on the vast Han sands. The withered grass of the Great Wall is completely barren. Pointlessly boast of the same race with wax color. Ashamed to see the sunflower flattering the sun. After the chaos, heads are all precarious. New labels and names are dignified and grand. Dragon flags and imperial robes are all child's play. What emperor is like Shi Jingtang?

Green Recalls Past Travels

Pond grass grows, and frogs croak noisily. Five hundred weeping willows house the jade city. Ten thousand points of misty light weigh heavy on the donkey's back. A river of spring water is as light as duckweed. Watch the light rain from the pavilions on the mountaintop. In the mirror, the clouds and sky flatter the early dawn. Dividing the indigo snail mountain is useless. Leave it for another life to write the wondrous Lotus Sutra.

Blue Because Green is not a True Color, Rewriting This

Your robe and my temples resonate with each other. The bamboo courtyard's incense is exceptionally clear. The lake after rain and clearing sky is one color. Wind passes over the field in a thousand layers of waves. Open the wine, and Ruan Ji casts starry eyes. Go to the tomb, and Feng Niang remembers small names. Always remember the willow shade and fragrant grassy land. Artemisia mud dumplings pass Qingming.

Black Mourns Today

Scribbled graffiti is always disliked for being faint. Gray hairs are dyed, and the color never thickens. Pulling strings behind the scenes is all close to ink. Giving charcoal in the snow, how can it be red? Fish squirt liquid to escape easily. Evil spirits spew sand and shoot shadows skillfully. Not seeing, not hearing is not easy. Sleeping country ant dreams are still layered.

White Praises Gandhi

The bright autumn paulownia washes the sun. Pointlessly compare invincibility to King Qi. Drying salt and washing the sea are a thousand layers of snow. Scattered pastures and ten thousand points of sheep. Empty room ascetic generates wondrous thoughts. Cloth-clad prime minister has radiance. Mangdang's red emperor, dragon and snake fight. The ghost mother cries at night, temples with frost.

Five Colors

Only radiance generates brilliance. Dragons soar, and phoenixes gather, filling the distant sky. Watch the first sun from the mountaintop clouds. The setting sun hangs on the building's corner, broken rainbow. Weaving maids sit at looms, cutting strange brocades. Nüwa refines stones to mend the azure dome. Do not be surprised at the dazzling strangeness. The world-cleansing articles are fundamentally different.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Five: Tearful Faces See Off Those Departing Home for Distant Frontier Garrisons, Wind and Sand Thoroughly Blocking the Nighttime Departure to Station in a Lonely City

In the face of wind and sand, the east was already somewhat fish-belly-colored, and a half-circle of earthen fort could be seen in the distance, discovered in a mountain depression. On the earthen fort, there was also a three-story watchtower, standing out in the sky, which made this area of mountaintops with scattered trees have a different flavor. Looking at the castle, it stood quietly between the valleys, and there was no movement to be seen. Everyone's breathing seemed to shorten, staring at the mountain fort, just walking towards it. Arriving at the edge of the castle, they saw that the two doors of the fort were wide open, and a villager leading a camel was coming out from inside. Seeing this large group of soldiers with guns and knives walking up, he panicked, dropped the rope, and turned around to run into the castle. Bao Fang looked at the castle dozens of steps away, and ordered the army to stop, but called Zi Qiang to his side and said to him: Company Commander Zhao, take two brothers into the fort, explain our intentions to the fort leader, and then we will enter. Zhao Zi Qiang agreed, unwilling to take more people. Apart from two accompanying soldiers, he only let Sergeant Wang Qili follow. Entering the fort, there were forty or fifty households inside, all houses made of yellow mud and sorghum stalks, with several short walls of messy stones surrounding the open space, clearly the foundations of houses that had collapsed long ago. The sky had just dawned, and it was a day of wind and sand, and the people in the fort had not yet gotten up. Zi Qiang said to Shi Li: This place is called Ping An Village, I only saw the name on the map. The brigade commander has ordered that this place is very important, the provincial army here does not care, and the enemy is very concerned, we must take over when everyone is caught off guard. It's fine to come, but the battalion commander is afraid of scaring the people, so he wants to give gifts before using force. Running here in such a hurry, where are we going to find the fort leader? Let's just randomly knock on a door, find a commoner and ask. Shi Li stood under a mud wall and heard someone inside the house say: It's still early, I'll sleep a little longer. (336)

Random Talk

Opening Remarks

— He Ru

Opening remarks are not found in the classics, "only seeing" these three words is the essence. The list of gods declares "precisely," so write good words in succession. The Journey to the West poem is the true original, not knowing the original intent and interpretation. The Seventeen Histories Romance is written by Sheng An, only because he was banished to Yunnan. The Book of the Four Books can be explained with bark, so humorous and widely circulated. Eternal sorrow comes from Yuan Gong's hand, who will completely continue it in the Qing Dynasty? Liu Ma Zi's single clap of the board rings, Mo Ling's autumn high song enters the spirit's end. Who can sing Double Phoenix Pearls? Who can play Three Smiles Fate? Who sang and played the South Tower Tale? Who adapted Jade Bracelet? Who newly wrote Romance of the West Chamber? Who composed the old White Peony? There's also Cui E privately gifting the Pearl Pagoda, but no Yu Er visiting the Emerald Garden three times. There are three hundred types of ballad ancient texts, singing one will take two or three years. Only opening remarks are easy to sing, nothing more than the Queen Mother and the Eight Immortals. Change the Southern lyrics into ten-character scores, a sealed memorial presented to the nine-layered heavens. Longevity opening remarks are vulgar and unbearable, only using a hundred longevities to celebrate the grand banquet. Happiness opening remarks are truly hilarious, only using a couple's happy reunion. New compilations have seen book music, bidding New Year's greetings on the old lunar New Year. Nine Harmony Advertising has a new method, lingering sounds spread everywhere. The editor is named Zhang Xunzi, a ballad veteran is Zhang Futian. Zhu Yaoxiang originally intended to issue, and there's also the storytelling master Zhou Yuquan. How many people know the figures in the book market, only a brief expression, not complete. Speaking of the opening remarks and singing method, unspeakably wonderful is in tuning the strings. The technique must be practiced for three years, explaining the work measurements of the four strings. Kong Yunting wants to score the Peach Blossom Fan, the Xiao Hu Lei music house must be transmitted first. As long as the pipa is played well, the magical desire reaches the tip of an autumn hair. I am an outsider, knowing that there is a separate sky in the pot. Only because a friend came to entrust, completing twenty articles overnight. Although not understanding the mystery, the gaming article is originally accidental. If vulgarity is called high quality, any wonderful sentence is overturned. Neither is it Immortal by the River, nor Partridge Sky, neither is it Silkworm Washing Brook Sands to seal words, nor does it resemble the tail sound changing to a minor key. Level tones and oblique tones are not the same as poetic sentences, and sound rhymes do not discuss the whole point of it all, as long as the Wu dialect sings round and round. Now the opening remarks are truly exquisite, a burst of pipa plays casually. Specifically speaking of stealing sound and changing breath, completing the song in eight or ten sentences. Not discussing the goodness or badness of the text, only the large dollar is in hand. Elder ballads had many skills, a full pearl ball was sung for three years. Who can match Ma Rufei's humor, Li Jinlou's pipa is wonderful like an immortal. The opening remarks and singing are all later generations, jokes and interjections are good at turning around. The West Chamber's initial opening remarks method, the pattern is newly turned by Lu Dan'an. Wore a Japanese robe and sang it for three whole years, the South Tower Tale only sang for one day. The entire Dream of the Red Chamber is not sung by anyone, the new drama has been performed in the Grand View Garden. I am now studying everything one by one, the first to pay attention to is miscellaneous articles. Adopt news as material, broadcasting intends to re-publicize. International news is transmitted opposite, financial market prices are in front. Domestically produced goods should be promoted, do not use entertainment to win people's joy. Beijing tunes are difficult to hire famous actors, phonograph records mix time. Beijing accent drum has a humorous fun, only the opening remarks put together a few articles. The east is not finished, the west is invited, Silver Star just goes up and then southeast. If it weren't for the car to take you, the pipa would be so busy that the strings would break. This is Shanghai's broadcasting business, it is difficult to say that the opening remarks are successful. It is not that the Wu dialect is inherently soft, you must speak the source of Chinese and foreign phonetics. Ouh, ya, chao, zha is difficult to listen to, do not learn the bird tongue of the southern barbarians. If you want to sing the national sound, people will naturally understand, concentrate on writing the opening remarks. Fortunately, there is not much to do during the New Year, sing the game opening remarks for the New Year. The ancients have words that must be remembered, you and I each spend our own year. You are not half-baked, I do not have such things. Everyone is spending a poor year, poor in not having large dollars. If you have something to say, friends are good, calling people to be deceived is against the heavens. I write the opening remarks originally without understanding, he publishes a special issue and wants capital. Singing and playing the opening remarks is eating, could it be that I can be a god? This is also a past word, who has time to eat dry white rice. Each person sweeps the snow in front of their own door, do not ask the Dragon King for water money. Ballads are mostly written by literati, the wonderful parts of opening remarks cannot be transmitted. Who twisted off people's voices, Yu Ming's Four Dreams record Linchuan? Whose pipa transmitted a different tune, seeing off guests at Xunyang, Bai Letian? Good opening remarks are truly rare, even if I forcefully revived Bai Ye, I would not say everything completely, boldly write the opening remarks.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Silver Prices and National Products

— Pan Yinge

Recently, the Chinese people have been promoting national products, and it can be said that they are sparing no effort. In good conscience, who wouldn't want to purchase and use national products? However, promotion is promotion, and the market for national products is still limited. Imports of foreign goods are still continuous. Even for Japanese goods alone, imports last year totaled 200 million yuan. What is the reason for this? As I see it, the biggest reason is that foreign goods are cheaper. It is a well-known fact that foreign goods are dumped. To know why the dumping of foreign goods in China can cause the prices of all goods to fall uniformly, there is a clever method in it. This method was first implemented by the British. On September 17, 1931, Britain suspended the redemption of gold pound banknotes. Therefore, the price of the Shanghai tael gradually became cheaper. As a result, British goods such as piece goods and cotton yarn seemed to be uniformly cheaper to the Chinese. As the shilling became cheaper day by day, British goods became cheaper day by day, and sales became more and more developed. The reason why Britain suspended redemption was due to the European financial crisis. (This European crisis triggered the September 18th Incident in the Northeast. If Europe had not had this crisis, there might not have been an incident in the Northeast.) Who knew that this would lead to the discovery of a new life in Eastern trade. Because at this time, Britain's business in China was being greatly encroached upon by Japan. Since the fall in the shilling, a way out has been found unintentionally. Truly, "a blessing in disguise." After Britain gained the benefit of the low shilling, the first to be envious was, of course, our noble neighbor. After the Seiyukai's Inukai Tsuyoshi cabinet came to power, it immediately suspended the redemption of gold yen banknotes. Half of this was due to financial reasons, and half was due to trade relations. Sure enough, since Japan suspended the redemption of gold yen, Japanese goods have been very cheap, even cheaper than British goods. This is an important reason why Japanese goods are imported in large quantities.

Since Britain and Japan have won in the Chinese market, Uncle Sam on the other side of the Pacific has been even more agitated. He feels that his gold dollar is really too expensive. In any case, the war debts cannot be cleared up for a while, and he is suffering losses in the short term, sacrificing his commercial interests in China first. Therefore, since President Roosevelt came to power, he has been singing a complete good show of suspending the redemption of gold dollars. The more the show is sung, the more energetic it becomes, and in the middle, a climax is added of uniting various countries to set a silver agreement to raise the price of silver. Readers, please think about what he is doing by lowering the gold dollar on the one hand and raising silver on the other? This is nothing more than wanting to promote cheap goods in China, which uses silver. Therefore, in the Northeast, our noble neighbor is using force to invade. For two years, the gongs and drums have been noisy, making a mess. However, in the West, a currency war has been raging. The amount of import surplus has opened a new chapter in the history of trade, reaching a huge amount of 700 million yuan. As I see it, 700 million yuan a year, 7 billion yuan in ten years, after ten years, even if China is peaceful, it will perish. In short, China today is completely the lean meat that others are chasing. (No longer fat) The desire to chase is endless, but China's flesh and blood are limited. The silver problem is the national product problem, it is the national life problem, how to deal with it properly is the responsibility of the leaders of all sectors of our country.

Women Promote Domestic Cloth

— Sun Choucheng

—Good News for the Women's National Products Year—

The Shanghai Native Cloth Shop in Penglai Market, Xiaoximen, Shanghai, was initiated by leaders such as the Shanghai County Education Bureau and the County Farmers Education Center. Its purpose is to promote genuine domestic native cloth, increase the income of farmers, and is different from those who specialize in profit. The farmers in Shanghai County, in addition to cultivating fields, all take spinning and weaving cloth as a side business. In recent years, luxury has become the fashion, and imported goods flood the market. The number of Chinese people using native cloth has gradually decreased. After the September 18th and January 28th incidents occurred one after another, the money market was extremely tight. The cloth shops in the countryside were unable to turn around, and they lacked funds to go to the countryside to buy native cloth, resulting in the goods that rural women had worked hard to weave day and night being unattended. Since the goods were stranded, they had no money to buy raw materials to spin and weave, and they all waited helplessly for death, with furrowed brows. The county authorities believed that the bankruptcy of the rural economy was not only related to the lives of farmers, but also affected the security of the entire county. Therefore, they made every effort to promote and improve it. In addition to holding native cloth exhibitions to promote it, they also established the China Cloth Clothing Association to encourage people to join the association and practice the declaration of saving the country with cloth clothing. In order to facilitate the improvement of native cloth, they also initiated the Native Cloth Improvement Association with comrades such as Pan Yangyao and Wang Zhixin of the China Textile Industry Society, and established a native cloth factory, and specially contracted weaving households, sent people to guide them, and provided them with raw materials to facilitate their work. Because the area near Penglai Market is full of schools, the uniforms of students have been adopted by the two education directors, Xu Peihuang and Pan Gongzhan, in a circular to use native cloth. Therefore, a store was set up here to promote sales. It is divided into a retail department and a clothing department. All the cloth samples include more than ten kinds, such as Free Wool, Zhongshan Wool, Peace Cloth, Herringbone Wool, Shame Cloth, and Cloud Brocade. The patterns are divided into thread reed, narrow reed, stripes, squares, and dice. The colors are red, white, gray, and blue. Because this year is the Women's National Products Year, Ms. Wang Zhuoqiu, a high-achieving student from the Wuxi Jingzhi Girls' School, was specially hired to promote sales. Ms. Wang once served as a staff member of the Ministry of Communications and the chief of the Certificate Issuance Section of the Wuhu Shipping Administration Bureau. She is known for her communication skills. She specially made a purple native cloth cheongsam, with black and white diagonal stripes around the edges. From a distance, it looks like Qing's foreign style, covered with a cotton wool short coat, black edges and silver buttons. She wears it to various schools to act as a mobile trademark and persuade students to purchase it. The schools that have already ordered it include dozens of schools such as Shanghai Girls' High School, Aiqun, Qingxin, Minli, Huiqun, Wuben, China, Huiling, Xunyu, Meixi, and Honglu. This is also good news for the Women's National Products Year.

Family and National Products

— Mu Yin

It's been more than a year since the Chinese people advocated national products. Last year was the National Products Year. Examining the results, even the four necessities of life, food, clothing, housing, and transportation, are still almost entirely foreign goods. I ask you, what kind of country is this? Therefore, if we don't want the country to perish, we must advocate national products and recover our rights!

The National Products Year has already passed, and the Women's National Products Year has just begun. Therefore, the sisters should make some achievements in this year's responsibility of advocating national products! However, men cannot therefore shirk their responsibility and arbitrarily use foreign goods. You must know that advocating national products is the duty of the people. If we work hard, China will be saved! Therefore, advocating national products is the best way to save ourselves and others!

In the Women's National Products Year, the sisters want to make some achievements. First, we should start with the entire family. Therefore, we want to talk about "Family and National Products."

We will not talk about anything else, but only about the ladies and young ladies in the general middle and upper class families in China. They are really a twelve-point authentic volunteer salespersons in clothing. Try to see if China does not have good silks and woolens? The silk crêpe of the American and Asian Silk Weaving Factory and the latest spring style Luo Na silk of 1923, the butterfly cloth and butterfly velvet of the Hongxinliang Weaving Factory, the exquisite woolens produced by the Zhanghua Woolen Textile Company, etc., are all very good clothing materials, but they not only do not want to use them, but they must wear foreign silk, foreign wool, and foreign velvet. As for daily toothpaste, hair growth oil, rouge, face powder, perfume, snow powder, and other things, there are also Chinese goods, and the products are very good, and they are not inferior to foreign goods, but they must buy foreign goods. And so on, all the utensils and furniture seem to be made of foreign raw materials, which are not enough to add to the spectacle. Because of this, foreign goods naturally flood into middle-class families as if it were a common thing. No matter how much you shout "advocate national products," if the women do not first shoulder this responsibility, China will not be able to sell its goods even if it has them. The more they cannot be sold, the more the national products industry will not be able to develop. Because the national products industry cannot develop, there is no power to improve it. In this way, the future of national products will always be hopeless. In short, advocating national products is not the responsibility of a few people. Everyone should do their best and cooperate to be effective. We expect the housewives of every family in China to take on the responsibility of advocating national products with great enthusiasm, and adhere to the principle of not using anything but national products, ten years as one day. In this way, not only can we refuse foreign goods to penetrate into people's daily life, but China may also be saved because of this! Dear sisters! Run to the top of the Women's National Products Year and work hard!

Shopping at the Market

— Du Yun

"Shopping at the market" is a colloquialism. Everyone who lives in the area near North Henan Road in this city and the nearby national products market understands this sentence. It means to take a stroll through the national products market. In Shanghai, where every inch of land is gold, it is not easy to live. Children hide in cages like chickens and have nowhere to spend their time. In summer, they are afraid of being exposed to the sun when they go out; in winter, they are afraid of being blown by the cold wind when they go out. For this reason, mothers generally take their children to play in the national products market, which is called "shopping at the market."

If women can take their children to shop at the market, not only can they solve the problem of children's entertainment, but also have a related relationship with advocating national products. In this Women's National Products Year, I specially present it to the female compatriots.

First, the national products market always welcomes anyone to visit. Then, when you go in to appreciate it, you can unintentionally make you recognize the names and styles of various national products.

Second, take the children to visit often, and buy some daily necessities by the way. You have bought genuine national products, and the children can develop the habit of loving national products. Fourth, shopping at the national products market more often will naturally buy more national products—and buy less foreign goods. Now, just based on the small consumption of our family, we have traded more than ten yuan in the short period of three or two months. If we consider the residents near the market with a thousand families, then the minimum transaction should be 10,000 or 20,000 yuan. This can be said to be advocating national products.

Finally, I would like to add a sentence that in addition to the national products market on North Henan Road mentioned here, there are also several national products markets on Nanjing Road, and there are also places that specialize in selling national products in various places. I also ask female compatriots to take the opportunity to visit more often.

The Manufacture of Bakelite

— Ma Yipiao

Recently, the buy-one-get-one-free or buy-one-get-two-free bakelite and bakelite jade items in major national products markets of companies on Nanjing Road have really broken the sluggishness of this winter, and the market has been very lively for a while. Their colors are really lovely; especially the jade-like color of bakelite jade is much more elegant than glass! A year ago, bakelite jade was almost not seen, but now, everyone knows it and uses it, but what is their celestial body? There are still many people who don't know; so I'm here to introduce it, I will first talk about bakelite, then talk about bakelite jade.

Bakelite, also known as phenolic plastic, was originally named Bakelite. It was successfully improved by the American Bakeland and has been around for 23 or 24 years. Now all countries can manufacture it, and there are more than a dozen names. Our country's Shengde Company can also manufacture it.

The main raw materials of bakelite are Carbolic acid and Formalin. The manufacturing method is to heat equal amounts of carbolic acid and formalin with an alkaline condensation agent (such as Ammonia) for several hours, which will separate into two layers, the upper layer is water, and the lower layer is the initial condensate of bakelite. The condensate is liquid or solid, soluble in alcohol or acetone (Acetone), brittle, and melts when heated, just like rosin. If it is heated again, it becomes a hard solid that no longer dissolves in solvents. However, if the solid is placed in a mold and heated and pressed appropriately, it can be pressed into products, and the solid will eventually become an irreversible substance that no longer dissolves and no longer melts. It can resist ordinary acids and bases, and can withstand heat up to 300 degrees Celsius. Especially, the fact that it does not conduct electricity at all is its characteristic, so it can be said to be the most suitable material for electrical materials.

The bakelite raw material used for bakelite products is mixed with pigments and sawdust or asbestos before the condensate becomes solid, and then crushed into powder after it is condensed, commonly known as Bakelite Moulding Powaer.

The bakelite powder is placed in a steel mold, heated to about 160 degrees Celsius, and pressed with a press to obtain the products seen on the market.

The production of bakelite powder is the largest in the United States, with an annual output of 80 million yuan, followed by Germany and England. In the future, the use will be expanded and developed without limit, which can also be regarded as the glorious contribution of synthetic chemistry.

Two Questions Raised by the Women's Circle

— Yang An

How to Satisfy People? How to Easily Distinguish?

Everyone knows that domestic goods should be promoted and used, but the most difficult problem is that it is difficult to distinguish between the genuine and the fake. Mrs. Cai Yuanpei first raised this question at a reception at the Brahma Wangdu Club, saying that consumers clearly want to buy domestic goods, but because they lack the ability to distinguish, they are deceived, which inevitably leads to disappointment. Then, Ms. Wang Xiaoying, representing the women's circle, raised two points: First, how to make the products satisfactory? Second, how to prevent domestic goods from being confused with non-domestic goods? Finally, Mrs. Pan Gongzhan, Ms. Lin Kecong, also made sincere statements on several points such as improving domestic goods, distinguishing domestic goods, and recognizing domestic goods. The next day at the Lake Society meeting, Mr. Cai Jie Min and Mr. Huang Renzhi also expressed these opinions, so I will come here to explain it, perhaps to answer the opinions raised by everyone:

It is difficult to run a business, and it is even more difficult to run a domestic goods business. The leaders of general factories work hard to improve their products every day, but they still cannot satisfy many people. This is certainly related to technology and economy, but the psychological effect is also very important. To be fair, if you go to a domestic goods company to take a look, Chinese domestic goods, not to mention the rapid progress, even the increase in variety is amazing and admirable. If those who buy domestic goods study carefully, most domestic goods can replace foreign goods and even surpass them. Even if the price is more expensive and the color is worse, it is very gratifying that a nascent industrial country can do this. If you have a strong spirit of sacrifice and determination, and trust the domestic goods company, you can use it as much as possible without doubt.

Speaking of distinguishing, it is certainly necessary to rely on the consumer's own eyesight, but this responsibility should be borne by the domestic goods company to first review the products. If there is any doubt, in any case, they should not sell it for him. Since consumers have completely entrusted the distinguishing procedure to the domestic goods company, then how cautious and strict the domestic goods company should be to fulfill its national duty. General customers can also rest assured. At the same time, I hope that the National Government will quickly implement the regulations on the marking of domestic goods as scheduled, and no longer hesitate. And the general traders who steal the sky and change the day should also take out their conscience, repent and change their minds, and no longer do things that confuse the fake with the genuine to deceive and harm people. A quarter of the Women's Domestic Goods Year has passed, how hard should everyone work!

Believe It or Not

— Xi Yin

If any high-ranking official can personally know how to wear local goods, then those below will surely follow suit! Let's look at the past: The Qin Dynasty was extravagant and the Han Dynasty was simple. The Han Dynasty was well governed, and there were many elders' behaviors. The Sui Dynasty was extravagant and the Tang Dynasty was simple. The Tang Dynasty was well governed, and brocade embroidery was useless. I think if the current National Government officials also become simple like the Han and Tang Dynasties, and their governance is good, then foreign goods will be useless.

Not to mention high-ranking officials, even if someone with a little reputation rises up and does it, those below will surely follow suit. A Chu person flaunted his clothes, and someone wore extra-thick clothes and liked black cloth. The villagers all followed suit, silk did not enter the border, and the dyeing workers moved far away. I think if the current county magistrate or provincial chairman also likes domestic cloth like the Taipu, then at least the people in one county or one province will follow suit, and foreign goods will not enter the border and move far away.

Not to mention people with a reputation, even if a commoner can rise up and do it, the villagers can also follow suit. Chen Youliang's father liked to wear coarse clothes. When he broke through Qi, he did not kill those who wore coarse clothes. A merchant from Luo was in Qi, and was spared because he wore coarse clothes. He returned and wore coarse clothes for the rest of his life, and the villagers all followed suit, silk did not enter the border, and the dyeing workers moved far away. I think if anyone now wears domestic cloth for the rest of their lives like the merchant from Luo, the villagers may also follow suit, and foreign goods will never enter the border again.

The Principal's Daughter

— Han Yu

The New Year holiday is over, and the students who went home have returned to school. On the public notice board, I saw a very strange notice:

"This afternoon at 4:00 p.m., our school will hold a girls' talk. All female students are expected to attend! This notice is from the Principal's Office." At that time, many people speculated that it might be for the New Year's Eve party.

At 4:00 p.m., the auditorium was full of girls. They were eager to know the meaning of the talk, and were all looking at the entrance. After a while, they saw the principal's daughter slowly walking to the stage from the entrance, which had already surprised them all. What surprised them even more was that the principal's daughter was not wearing her glamorous clothes today, but a blue cloth cheongsam, and she did not apply any powder on her face.

The principal's daughter was originally the school beauty of that school. Her purpose of studying was only to pass. After passing, she would never study that subject again. What she paid most attention to was decoration. From her head, face, body, to her feet, there was nothing she didn't want to compete with the girls in the whole school. In terms of qualifications and decoration, she almost became the leader of all the female students. The female students in the school tried their best to dress newer and more beautifully than her, but no one could beat her. Today, she is so undecorated, of course, this surprised them all.

The principal's daughter went to the podium and began to speak: "Everyone may be surprised, why has my decoration changed like this today? In fact, I can tell you all, this is my new life! Today I can tell you all the process of my new life: On New Year's Day, I went to participate in the Women's Friendship Conference. The purpose of my participation was actually meaningless. But at that conference, I was greatly moved. Therefore, I got a new life. What is my new life? It is to use domestic goods! My purpose of using domestic goods is to save China! We use foreign goods for the sake of beauty. But how can the price of beauty compare to patriotism? Can't we use the same domestic goods to replace them? Even if domestic goods have shortcomings compared to foreign goods, can't we slightly damage our beauty for the sake of patriotism? Now I have got a new life, I hope everyone will also get the same new life!" Then there was a burst of applause.

The principal's daughter said again: "I have already prepared a list, which can now be distributed to you all. The list lists the names of domestic goods that can replace foreign goods. You can buy excellent domestic goods according to the names on the list. And I hope that from today onwards, we will all switch to domestic goods. For the foreign goods you bought before, you can either discard them, or switch to domestic goods after you use them up. Only in this way can we fulfill the responsibility of women in the Women's Domestic Goods Year. After the principal's daughter announced the end of the meeting, everyone returned to the dormitory. Most of them sealed up the foreign goods and put them in a room, with the words "Memorial of Regret for Using Foreign Goods" written on the outside for the male students to visit. In this way, the male students also gradually switched to domestic goods.

Two weeks later, everyone in the whole school, except for the indispensable foreign goods that cannot be replaced, switched to domestic goods. Everyone said: "Like the principal's daughter, she is qualified to be a leader!"

Huang Jianzhong Proposes to Improve Higher Education

Seeking Substantive Improvement

(Nanjing, 14th) Huang Jianzhong, Acting Director of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, told reporters on the 14th that higher education in our country should seek substantive improvement, not an increase in quantity. School equipment should be strengthened and enriched, the level should be improved, and the employment prospects for graduates are particularly important issues. Now it is not easy for university graduates to find other jobs. In the future, they should be directed to social occupations.

Jiangsu

Education Delegation

—Observations in Nagasaki—

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education previously sent Zhou Hou Shu, Principal of Yangzhong School, Cao Chu, Principal of Zhenshi School, Yan Liyang, Principal of Xuzhong School, Teng Songshi, Principal of Huangdu Normal School, Shen Shanzhi, Principal of the Attached Elementary School of Zhenshi School, Sheng Langxi, Principal of Shangzhong Experimental Elementary School, Zhao Hongqian, Curator of Zhenjiang People's Education Center, and Yu Jiwen, a teacher from Zhenjiang Teachers School, who went with them, to form the Jiangsu Provincial Education Delegation to Japan for inspection by boat on the 28th of last month. They arrived in Nagasaki at 1:00 p.m. on March 1st. The details have been recorded in previous reports. Now, the letter from the delegation is recorded below.

(Omitted above) Arrived in Nagasaki at 1:00 p.m. on March 1st. After landing, they visited two schools, one was the Mitsubishi Private Vocational School, and the other was the Nagasaki Prefectural Women's Normal School. From these two schools, they felt that there were many things that could be learned from them, such as the cleanliness of the entire school layout, the hard work of the students' operations, and the students' bowing to the visitors. The Mitsubishi Vocational School is divided into shipbuilding and machinery departments, and the level is the same as that of middle school. After graduation, they serve in the Mitsubishi Shipyard. Usually, the internship is also in the factory. When students are in the internship, the factory will give them wages. First-year students get 20 cents a day, second-year students get 30 cents, and third-year students get 50 cents. Students in the school wear extremely crude yellow cloth uniforms, and although the weather is very cold, the clothes are very thin. They are barefoot all day long, without shoes and socks. The strength of their physical resistance can be seen. When the teacher enters the classroom at a fixed time, a student shouts "Attention", and the whole body stands up and salutes. Usually, they are very respectful and obedient to the teacher. Physical exercise focuses on martial arts and wrestling. The women's school is prefectural, and its equipment has surpassed our provincial schools. There are 365 students in the whole school, and 250 boarders. All the cleaning matters of the whole school are handled by the students in rotation. They pay great attention to household affairs and etiquette training. In terms of household affairs, there is a laundry room, and the clothes are washed by the students themselves. The cement laundry pool is well equipped and can be imitated. The cooking practice room is equipped with multiple cement platforms, each equipped with a Western-style gas stove and a Japanese firewood stove. The sewing room is equipped with more than a dozen Singer sewing machines, and there is also a handmade sewing room. In terms of etiquette training, there is an etiquette practice room, decorated with family style, where students practice family etiquette and hold tea parties. There is also a large reception room for students to communicate with each other and learn etiquette. Students bow and salute to the image of Emperor Showa every morning when they enter the school and before meetings. A shrine is enshrined in the dining hall, and they salute before picking up chopsticks. The students' attitude is very leisurely and quiet. Within ten minutes after class, it is also very quiet and orderly, unlike the noisy situation of students in general schools in our country. The students are all very strong and full of energy. From this, we can see the strength of their physique. The school is equipped with classrooms for each subject, such as literature classrooms, history and geography classrooms, science and chemistry classrooms, and nature classrooms. The school's books for each subject are placed in each special classroom. There is no special person to manage them, but the layout is very neat, and there is no fear of loss. In this way, books can be fully utilized. The items sold in the school store are listed outside, and the manager sits inside, only responsible for collecting money and accounting, unlike our country's setting up counters, which is a natural gap between buyers and sellers. The students' spirit of autonomy can be seen from this. The most admirable and most worthy of imitation of its equipment is the local product display room—there are three rooms of the same size as the classrooms, one is the geography display room, one is the history display room, and the other is the nature display room. The items displayed in them are all local products of Nagasaki Province collected by the students themselves. The geography room displays all agricultural and industrial products of this province and charts, books, etc. related to the geography, humanities, and climate of this province. The history room displays portraits of historical figures in this province, hanging pictures of important historical facts, and models, charts, and books of costumes and cultural relics of past dynasties. The nature room displays plant wax leaves collected by students themselves, taxidermy animal specimens, and various mineral specimens, all limited to those owned by this province. Among them, pearls, crystals, tortoiseshells, etc., which are famous products of Nagasaki, are especially beautiful. The items displayed in the three rooms are dazzling and breathtaking, making people sigh. It is not easy for our provincial middle schools to get this. Zhou, the director of the Provincial Department of Education in this province, intends to vigorously promote local education. The intention is very good. In the future, all counties and schools should earnestly imitate it. If not, students will not know the loveliness of their hometown. Those who do not love their hometown do not even know where to start loving their country. Moreover, this can make them know all the raw materials and production in this province, which can inspire their interest in engaging in production. Moreover, everything is collected, produced, and arranged by the students, which is especially meaningful.

When visiting, the most shocking thing is that in the reading room of the women's normal school students, there is a large, carefully framed character hanging, which reads "Defeat the Enemy Country" in four big characters. Seeing it makes people tremble and their hair stand on end. In addition, the walls of Mitsubishi Public School are hung with portraits of generals after the Russo-Japanese War. Everywhere shows their imperialist ambition of aggression. (Omitted below)

Jiangsu Provincial School Funding

Payment Notice Signed

Half a Month's Payment Will Be Made Soon

The payment notice for the second half of February and the first half of March for the Jiangsu Provincial Rural Normal Schools and Provincial Elementary Schools (the full month of February for Social Education Institutions and Vocational Schools, and the first half of February for Middle Schools and Normal Schools) has been signed by the Jiangsu Education Fund Auditing Committee. At the same time, the payment notice for the spring study abroad expenses has also been signed and will be sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education for stamping soon. It is heard that the payment notice for one month's expenses for each school can be issued for half a month first, because the Jiangsu Education Treasury currently has 210,000 yuan. After deducting 100,000 yuan due on March 20 to repay the Jiangsu branches of the Bank of Communications, the remaining 110,000 yuan still needs to be raised by 30,000 to 40,000 yuan to be enough to pay half a month's expenses for the provincial schools. This City Will Review All Middle Schools

Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civic Education Teachers

The Review Committee Will Hold Its First Meeting Today

Since the Ministry of Education changed the Party Principles course in various schools to Civics, the central government believes that the content of the Civics course is related to the principles of our party, and the nature is still important. Therefore, it immediately ordered the Party Departments and Education Bureaus of various provinces and cities to end the previous committee for reviewing Party Principles teachers and establish a committee for reviewing the qualifications of deans of students and civics teachers to engage in qualification review to be careful about teachers. After the Party and government authorities in this city were issued the regulations, they immediately appointed Zhu Jiarang, Chen Bai, Zhu Yakui, Yu Zhongbiao, Jiang Wenbao, and five others as committee members. They also formed a committee with two ex officio members, Tong Hangbai and Pan Gongzhan, to be responsible for this matter, and decided to convene the first meeting today for progress. It is heard that this review of deans of students and civics teachers is limited to middle schools. Elementary school teachers do not need to apply. If there is no dean of students in a middle school, then the director of teaching in charge of moral education should also apply for review. Now, the regulations for the two subjects are transcribed below.

Regulations for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students in Middle Schools

Passed by the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the 4th Central Executive Committee on August 31, 1933

Article 1 The review of the qualifications of deans of students in middle schools nationwide shall be carried out by the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers in accordance with these regulations.

Article 2 The dean of students referred to in these regulations refers to the current or aspiring dean of students or director of teaching as stipulated in the middle school regulations.

Article 3 All deans of students and directors of teaching in middle schools nationwide shall be subject to review by the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers. Those who have not been reviewed or have failed the review three months after the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers in the area begins its work shall not continue to serve.

Article 4 The dean of students or director of teaching in middle schools nationwide shall apply to the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers or be requested by (1) middle schools, (2) educational administrative organs at all levels, or (3) party departments at all levels to request review.

Article 5 Any party member (including probationary party members) or person who has not yet joined the party but has studied the Three Principles of the People and has the qualifications of a middle school teacher stipulated by the educational administrative organ and has served in moral education in middle schools may request to be reviewed for the qualifications of a dean of students in various middle schools.

Article 6 Any applicant for review shall submit the various proofs of qualifications stipulated in Article 5 of these regulations, as well as the following documents: 1. Two recent half-length photos of themselves; 2. A letter of application; 3. A curriculum vitae.

Article 7 Party members with one of the following qualifications may be exempted from review, but must submit documents proving their qualifications to the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers for registration. After registration, they will obtain the qualifications of a dean of students in middle schools. 1. Obtained a certificate of qualification for the examination or review of deans of students in middle schools and have more than one year of experience in moral education in middle schools; 2. Served as a member of the Committee for Examining or Reviewing Party Principles Teachers and have experience in moral education in middle schools; 3. Currently serving or have served as a member of the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Education Teachers.

Article 8 The Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers shall issue a certificate of qualification to the deans of students who have passed the review and have the qualifications stipulated in Article 7 of these regulations.

Article 9 If there is a shortage of personnel with the qualifications stipulated in Article 5 and Article 7 of these regulations in various places, the principal of the school may propose to hire a person who has a definite understanding and belief in Party Principles, has definitely studied and has experience in moral education, and has the qualifications of a teacher stipulated by the educational administrative organ to the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers, stating the reasons. After approval, they will be a substitute dean of students.

Article 10 Before hiring a substitute dean of students, each middle school must submit the substitute dean of students' letter of application, curriculum vitae, school graduation certificate, or other documents sufficient to prove their educational qualifications, and two recent half-length photos. If they have written works, they should also submit the works together for review and approval, and a certificate of substitute dean of students will be issued before they can be hired.

Article 11 The Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers may ask two members of the Provincial or Special City Party Department to introduce the dean of students or substitute dean of students who has passed the review as probationary party members.

Article 12 After being hired by the school, the dean of students or substitute dean of students who has passed the review shall report their work status to the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers at least once every semester for assessment.

Article 13 If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee may propose amendments to the Central Executive Committee.

Article 14 These regulations shall be implemented upon the decision of the Central Executive Committee.

Regulations on the Qualification of Civic Education Teachers in Secondary Schools under Review

Passed by the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Fourth Central Executive Committee on August 31, 1933

Article 1: The qualification review for civic education teachers in all secondary schools across the country shall be conducted by the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers, in accordance with these regulations. The organization of the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers shall be separately determined.

Article 2: The term "civic education teacher" as used in these regulations refers to teachers who are currently teaching or voluntarily applying to teach civic education courses in various secondary schools.

Article 3: All civic education teachers in secondary schools across the country shall be subject to the review of the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers. Those who have not been reviewed, or who have been reviewed and found unqualified, within three months after the commencement of work of the respective Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers, shall not be allowed to continue in their positions.

Article 4: Civic education teachers in secondary schools across the country shall directly apply to the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers for review, or the review may be initiated by (1) various secondary schools, (2) educational administrative authorities at all levels, (3) Party headquarters at all levels.

Article 5: Any member of the Party (including probationary members) or any person who has not yet joined the Party but has studied the Three Principles of the People may apply for qualification review to become a civic education teacher in a secondary school, provided that they possess one of the following qualifications: 1. Graduates who have studied social sciences in specialized schools or above; 2. Those who possess the qualifications of secondary school teachers as stipulated by the educational administrative authorities and have taught social science subjects; 3. Those who possess the qualifications of secondary school teachers as stipulated by the educational administrative authorities and have indeed studied social science subjects and have written works.

Article 6: Applicants for review shall submit the various certifying documents of the qualifications stipulated in Article 5 of these regulations, and shall also submit the following items: 1. Two recent half-length photos of themselves; 2. A letter of intent; 3. A resume.

Article 7: Party members who possess one of the following qualifications may be exempted from review, but must submit documents proving their qualifications to the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers for registration, and then obtain the qualification of a civic education teacher in a secondary school: 1. Those who have obtained the certificate of qualification for Party Principles teachers in secondary schools through examination or review and have at least one year of teaching experience in secondary schools; 2. Former members of the Qualification Review Committee for Party Principles Teachers, and have served as teachers in secondary schools; 3. Those who are currently serving or have served as members of the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers.

Article 8: Civic education teachers who have passed the review and possess the qualifications stipulated in Article 7 of these regulations shall be granted a certificate of qualification by the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers.

Article 9: In areas where there is a shortage of personnel with the qualifications stipulated in Articles 5 and 7 of these regulations, the principals of the respective schools may propose to hire individuals who have a firm understanding and belief in Party Principles, have conducted in-depth research and have experience in civic education, and who meet the teacher qualifications stipulated by the educational administrative authorities. They shall state the reasons to the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers, and, upon approval, may serve as substitute civic education teachers.

Article 10: Before hiring a substitute civic education teacher, each secondary school must submit the substitute civic education teacher's letter of intent, resume, school diploma or other documents sufficient to prove the teacher's qualifications, and two recent half-length photos. If there are written works, they should be submitted together. Only after the review is passed and a certificate of qualification for substitute civic education teachers is granted, can they be hired.

Article 11: Civic education teachers and substitute civic education teachers who are not Party members but have passed the review may be introduced as probationary Party members by two members of the Provincial or Special Municipality Party Headquarters on behalf of the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers.

Article 12: Civic education teachers and substitute civic education teachers who have passed the review and have been hired by the school shall report their work situation to the Qualification Review Committee for Principals in Charge of Student Affairs and Civic Education Teachers at least once per semester for evaluation.

Article 13: If these regulations are not exhaustive, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee may propose amendments to the Central Executive Committee.

Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.

The Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee Decides

To Convene a Conference of Sports Supervisors from Various Provinces and Cities

To Pass Methods for Determining Physical Education Assessment Standards

Each Province Should Select a Normal School to Establish a Physical Education Department

Items for Report

(Nanjing, 14th) The Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education held its eleventh regular meeting at 9:00 AM on the 14th. Wang Shijie, Duan Xipeng, Zhang Boling, Wu Yunrui, Cheng Dengke, Wang Zhengting, Shen Siliang, Chu Minyi, Hao Gengsheng, and nineteen others attended the meeting, with Wang Shijie as chairman.

Hao Gengsheng reported on the proposed methods for determining the qualifications of physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools, unifying the application of national health education materials, running national summer physical education refresher courses, rewarding domestic sports products, and implementing methods for awarding sports medals and certificates. Members have already been assigned to draft these proposals, or they are currently being reviewed by the Ministry of Education. Shen Siliang and others reported on the preparations for participating in the Far Eastern Games.

Resolutions on Various Cases

The following resolutions were made: (1) The original proposal for national martial arts teaching materials standards for all levels of schools will be designated as provisional standards. The country will be divided into several regions, and a number of schools will be designated for experimentation. In the future, revisions will be made based on the experimental reports. 2. Regarding the proposal to invite physical education directors from various provinces and cities to come to Nanjing for a meeting to formulate work standards and methods for allocating funds, the resolution was: A. The Ministry of Education should issue an order to all provinces and cities to establish physical education supervisors and include the funding in the next year's budget. B. All provinces and cities should issue an order to send physical education supervisors to the summer physical education schools when they are opened, to hold meetings to discuss national physical education administration matters. 3. A uniform regulation for athletes should be established for all levels of schools nationwide. It will be submitted for discussion at the next meeting after revision. 4. The method for determining physical education assessment standards was revised and passed. If local physical education experts have any opinions, they can add testing items as they see fit and report the test results to the committee for reference. 5. Regarding the summer physical education school proposal, it was resolved that the drafting committee should revise it and promptly submit it to the Ministry of Education for promulgation and implementation, and preparations should be made as soon as possible. 6. Each province in the country should select one school from the provincial normal schools and add a physical education department to cultivate primary school physical education teachers suitable for the province. It was resolved to pass the proposal and request the Ministry of Education to order the education departments of each province to comply.

The United States Wins the Men's Championship

China Suffers a Miserable Defeat by One Point, 38 to 37, Yesterday

The Chinese Women's Team is Promising, Winning Again Against the Federation

The Previous Champion, Great Britain, Was Defeated by the United States Yesterday

The men's championship of the 9th Shanghai International Basketball Tournament has fallen into the hands of the United States. Although the Federation is composed of troops from many countries, it is not an opponent of China. It lagged behind China all the way and never managed to raise its head. Unexpectedly, in the last quarter, taking advantage of the Chinese team's adjustment, the Federation launched a fierce attack, scoring nine consecutive points, almost being caught up. The result was 34 to 32.

Dong Hua Scores Seven to One

Yesterday Soundly Defeated the British Navy

The Navy Collapsed in the Last Ten Minutes

A Scene from the Western League A Group Football Match

Dong Hua played against the British Navy at the Chinese baseball field yesterday and soundly defeated them, with a score of seven to one. This was a scene from the Western League A Group football match. The score was two to one in the first half. The Navy stubbornly resisted until the last ten minutes, when they were defeated beyond repair. Their goalkeeper's performance was unique. There were only a few hundred spectators.

The Navy Opens the Scoring First The Navy kicked off, and its momentum was not weak. The Dong Hua lineup was greatly burdened. Dong Hua's counterattack was ruined by inaccurate shots. After fifteen minutes, the Navy came to harass again, directly approaching the goal. Fortunately, a corner kick was saved. Davis opened it, and the landing point was accurate. Without any intention, Hale and Hantesheng rushed in, and by the time the goalkeeper knew, the ball had already rushed in.

Dong Hua Launches a Major Counterattack After losing first, Dong Hua launched a full-scale counterattack, ordering the siege of the Navy goal. The ball was like a cannonball, and despite the Navy goalkeeper's experience and the lack of shooting preparation, they were unable to score. At this time, the ball was in the middle zone. Dai saw that there was room for maneuver and was far to the right, so he could make a sneak attack. So he passed the ball to the right, and Yu Tian flew to hit the left corner diagonally, and happened to enter the goal, making the score 1 to 1. Fifteen minutes later, Wan Xianghua shot directly at the goal from the left corner. The ball bounced off the crossbar, and Li Rong'an kicked it in, making the score 2 to 1 in the first half.

The Last Thirty Minutes Starting in the second half, Dong Hua continued to use the encirclement strategy, going back and forth in front of the goal. Zhou Guangzhong was frustrated by repeatedly failing to score, and became very brave, scoring two consecutive goals, making the score 4 to 1. At this point, there were only ten minutes left in the game. The Navy defended desperately and did not come out again. Dong Hua attacked fiercely and did not rest. Wan Xianghua passed the ball in, and Dai Linjing got it with one strike, 5 to 1. Chen Yu Tian picked the ball over the goalkeeper and happened to fall into the goal, 6 to 1. Li Rong'an added another goal, 7 to 1. In these last ten minutes, the Navy collapsed beyond repair, which was also unexpected.
