Free Talk

Peach Blossom River is a Beauty's Nest

—Wo Ding

"Peach Blossom River is a beauty's nest..." This is a famous song of modern times, sung everywhere. Peach Blossom River is in Yiyang, Hunan. Does it mean that the most beautiful women in China come from there, because of the good scenery? Or is it for other reasons?

The people of Hunan are a very barbaric race, less civilized than Sichuan or Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and naturally combative. But because of their combative nature, most of the revolutionaries and counter-revolutionaries everywhere are from Hunan. So, for the creation of this Republic of China, the people of Hunan have contributed a lot of strength.

However, when many modern men and women hum this song lightly, how can they know the great suffering in it? Aren't the people of Hunan fighting outside all year round? "Poor bones lie by the endless river; yet still in her chamber, she dreams of her dear one." These two lines of poetry perfectly describe this current situation. Now, in the Peach Blossom River basin, or, more broadly, in the river basins of Xiang, Zi, Yuan, and Li, most of the men are dead bones, and countless women are still dreaming, hoping that their men will return as officials, or have a chance to live.

Whether war should exist is not a matter for discussion here. But this current situation is worth noting. The people are born like weeds and die like weeds. There is no need to talk about those who have died, because the theory of reincarnation is ultimately just a distant tale, but what about the so-called "survivors"? What methods can be used to eliminate or reduce this great amount of "human suffering"—poverty, helplessness, and misery? Raising them! Teaching them! Building them! Can this reduce even a hair's breadth?

This current situation is the same everywhere, but it is particularly obvious in Hunan. At this time, if there is someone who can "read the atmosphere", he should see black air everywhere, endless poverty, desolation, and grief! But we are happy to sing "Peach Blossom River is a beauty's nest"! ... And it has even been arranged into a Western dance tune! Dancing is actually good, and beauty is also good, but it might be even better if men didn't become "bones by the endless river"! "Transcendence" is also good, and performing Buddhist rituals is also fine, but instead of paying attention to the afterlife of the dead, it would be better to pay a little attention to the lives of the living!

Wooden Fish

— Bai Yan

From the narrow mountain path of Lotus Mountain, winding in, before you even walk a few dozen steps, you can see a towering temple. That is the Lotus Nunnery. Around the courtyard, dense bamboos grow thickly. When the sunlight filters the bamboo shadows onto the walls, it forms a natural pattern. The scenery is quite serene.

The temple only worships Guanyin, the Goddess of Mercy; besides her, there are some other deities. However, these deities are all in a "vassal" status. Inside the temple, besides an old nun, Jingxin, there is only a young nun, Huiming. In this desolate Lotus Nunnery, the master and disciple quietly spend their lonely days.

Huiming was sent to the nunnery from a young age. It is said that when Huiming was a child, her parents, greedy for the wealth of the village gentleman, Li, rashly betrothed their daughter to his son. However, less than two years after their engagement, the man died of "consumption." At that time, her husband's family did not make any proposals regarding her future, but her father believed that "a good horse doesn't eat returned grass, a good woman doesn't marry a second husband." It seemed that for a scholarly family like theirs, it would be quite shameful if their daughter could not remain faithful to one man until death, so they forcibly sent her to the nunnery.

For Huiming, when she was young, perhaps she could not bear the silence of the Buddhist temple: the dryness of vegetarian food: the hideous idols may have frightened her, but these were only limited to physical suffering. Spiritually, she was still content.

Later, in the mournful sound of the wooden fish, her age gradually increased. Now, she is a twenty-year-old young woman. Due to physiological changes, she gradually felt spiritual distress. Especially when she returned home to visit her family, seeing the joy of her younger brother and his wife and their eternal smiles, she felt deeply unhappy and acutely aware of her own desolation. She asked herself, "Why is this?" Thinking, tears welled up in her eyes…

At this moment, she sat cross-legged on the prayer mat, her palms joined in front of her chest. Following her master's chanting: and constantly striking the wooden fish. She glanced sideways at her master, seeing her looking down at the ground: at the same time, her shriveled lips were rapidly trembling. She lazily fixed her gaze on the wooden fish again. When the mallet struck it, a crisp sound was heard, which could be heard all the way down the mountain.

A lonely sound, a lonely life, woven into a net of sorrow; heavily shrouding her fragile heart. She was now faintly in a state of meditation. When she occasionally raised her head and caught a glimpse of the gold-plated bodhisattva in the shrine, her heart trembled even more violently. Hot tears streamed down her cheeks.

The sound of her striking the wooden fish gradually became dull.

Remembering the Great Golden Pagoda

— Yue Meng

On the train speeding towards Yangon, the first thing I saw rising high above the green foliage, giving travelers a smiling face from afar, was your figure, the Great Golden Pagoda! On the ship sailing from Yangon to the Indian Ocean, when I looked back and the outline of the metropolis had already disappeared, I suddenly saw you towering in the blue sky, as if reluctantly bidding farewell, and that was also your figure, the Great Golden Pagoda! I remember all of these, but what I will never forget is when, at dusk, the setting sun hung on your waist, and crows rose from the shade of the bodhi trees, scattering in the red sky of the evening, swirling into black stars, dancing around you, at this moment, seeing your languid appearance from afar, ah, how it makes people feel a sense of the rise and fall of empires! Or when I stroll along the banks of Green Lake at night, watching you covered in brilliant pearls, your soft golden reflection reflected in the lake, that expression full of the charm of a dancer going to a ball, how it makes people feel happy and delighted!

Now, at your feet, on the marble-paved path, are those grand scenes of offering flowers and incense still the same as they were back then? Are those good men and women in white clothes and floral skirts, whom I call gold worshippers, still singing and dancing below you during fine festivals, their interest undiminished from the past? Do you remember the tragic days when the monk U Wizaya, who advocated violent revolution and died on hunger strike in prison, was cremated by your side? Do you remember the days when the procession shouting "Simon go back" passed through the bustling city, circled to your feet, scattered into a sea of heads, and held demonstrations with prayers and speeches? Do you remember the great strike of five thousand Indian dockworkers, which turned the entire city into a bleak scene of death, and the incense and flowers there also showed an unprecedented dimness? Great Golden Pagoda, I remember all of these, and I miss them very much.

Please raise your head and look for me, are those thatched huts dotted in the golden rice fields still spewing blood-red crowns of fire and black columns of smoke? Are those brownish-yellow figures flashing in the green forests still holding up the white flags painted with gods and snakes? Great Golden Pagoda, which I have not seen for three years, please lift your toes and look for me.

On "Branding" (Continued)

— Mu Mutian

However, in recent years, the bankruptcy of Chinese rural villages has become more and more serious, and Zang Kejia will naturally notice this. However, due to a lack of social understanding, he failed to realistically sing about the lives of farmers in poetry. He sings about "refugees," "coal ghosts," "goddesses," "fishermen," "rickshaw pullers," "tavern waitresses," "fishmongers," etc., but he never grasped the lives and psychology of those people. He treats each image as a symbol, and describes it aesthetically. He shrouds the "refugees" in a decadent, dark atmosphere, without showing us their lives directly and realistically. He only gazes at them vaguely with his narrow humanitarianism. He does not indicate the relationship between the refugees and the collapse of the countryside. And in works such as "Old Horse," "Goddess," "Tavern Waitress," and "Fishmonger," he subjectively puts in his philosophy of stoicism. He does not objectively analyze their psychology based on those realistic images, but universally injects his own emotions into each of them. This is not realistic. In order to overcome this point, this young poet should abandon his empty and narrow philosophy, break open the hard shell of his small self, and do some solid work to study society's hardships. Because, unable to understand society, he sees pain and suffering as beautiful images, and says:

At the same time, you are afraid of overcoming it,

To be struck by a burst of emptiness from losing your opponent. ("Life")

This is an attitude of aestheticism. It is also because of this attitude that he depicts the "Coal Ghost" as a work of art:

Their faces are the night sky,

Sweat streams give it a Milky Way,

A pair of eyes radiating light,

Like two moons shining in the sky. ("Coal Ghost")

However, the poet's self-centered demands lead him to think conceptually of "strange heavenly fire." ("Heavenly Fire")

Lead him to think of "under the long wings of the night, there lies a bright dawn." ("Not long before that day.") Because he saw:

A young girl cannot get a meal,

Human flesh and pork are sold in the market the same. ("Heavenly Fire")

From miracles he thought of miracles. But what is a miracle?

Southern Journey Miscellany (Continued)

— Tang Tao

(5) New Year's Sundries

The inspector at the pier does not allow calendars combining the solar and lunar systems to land, and I cannot help but admire this. But here, even the director of the Public Security Bureau is busy making New Year's calls!

It is said that last year, the lunar calendar was not recognized here at all, and even New Year's greetings had to be whispered. Now, setting off firecrackers is a given, and some people even put up New Year couplets like "The Emperor's kindness is as vast as spring" on their doors!

Dragon boat lanterns are also one of the New Year's sundries. Each troupe has two dragon boat lanterns. At most, there are more than a dozen people, with all the stringed instruments and singing popular tunes. They can earn tens of thousands of coins a day. But this year, because the times are bad and there are many dragon boat lanterns, it is said that there will be some discounts.

Apart from dragon boat lanterns, the most common is the monk play. This only requires four or five children, each wearing a mask; three are monks, and one is a female pilgrim. From entering the temple to burn incense to the monks committing adultery, it can all be performed in two minutes. They perform this from house to house. The Fengyang flower drum has not been seen much in recent years, but it has been replaced by some heroes performing magic tricks. They swallow the sword into their stomach, leaving the hilt outside their mouth, shouting with their stomach straight. Once they receive the money, they pull out the sword and go to the next house. In addition, there are also tricks like playing horse lanterns and carrying the yellow dragon.

Another reason for the New Year's excitement should be gambling. Because on ordinary days, unless they are wealthy and powerful gentlemen, all gambling is strictly prohibited. But in the New Year, there are five days when people can indulge, which we call "Five Days of the King," meaning that in these five days, they can be as free as being crowned king.

The New Year is really a world for children. On New Year's Eve, they receive lucky money from their elders, and on New Year's Day, they put on brand new clothes, watch lanterns at home, and buy toys on the street. Even if poor children do not get these things, they can at least be scolded and beaten less.

In this respect, the lunar calendar may one day be abolished, but the children's happiness should be eternal.

A Tentative Translation of the Book of Songs

— Yu Shixia

The Rat

One

Look, the rat still has skin,

But he doesn't care about appearance.

He doesn't care about appearance,

What's the point of not dying?

Two

Look, the rat still has teeth,

But he doesn't care about face.

He doesn't care about face,

When is he waiting to die?

Three

Look, the rat still has limbs,

But he doesn't care about propriety.

He doesn't care about propriety,

Why doesn't he die quickly!

Book Talk (Continued)

— Shu

(3)

Based on the selfishness and secrecy of book collectors, as well as the disasters of war and fire, countless famous books and secret scripts are often permanently lost, which is a great regret. Therefore, on the other hand, "the crime of concealing books is greater than burning books." Li Qing (Yingbi) said: "Your younger brother has always thought that the crime of concealing books is greater than burning books. Truly seeing that once a book is concealed, it may be gnawed by rats, or damaged by silkworms and fish, or scattered by children and servants' windmills and thread books, if it is not passed on, it will be lost forever. Therefore, I sigh that the few volumes of Baopuzi can still be passed down to this day, not because of Bojie's secrecy in his tent, but because of the merit of those who took a few volumes from Bojie's tent. Your brother and I both want to be those takers, so we must borrow when we have books, copy when we borrow, and return when we copy. Rest assured, the promise will last forever, and it should be spread to all like-minded people. Be careful not to imitate Bojie's words, 'Only you and I share it, not spreading it widely.'" This opinion is extremely valuable. Only this method can make famous works and secret scripts be able to last forever in the world.

Dusk (5)

— Jin Yi

"Sister, why don't you stop, doing this will cause a headache again."

Qingsong raised her head, temporarily taking her pen away from the plain silk, her face suddenly showing a child-like joy, but it quickly disappeared, and she quietly replied:

"It's almost finished, when people are happy, they forget everything."

She smiled faintly, and Qingzhi walked over, looking at the Guanyin statue she was about to complete, outlined in light colors, the solemn and tranquil face of the Buddha, standing transcendently on a lotus petal.

"Isn't this considered finished?"

"The lotus petals haven't been colored yet, and I need to write a title."

She washed the used brush in the brush washer, mixed light pink, gently smeared it, and then used white water to depict the nearby areas even lighter. She used a brush to write the words "Qingsong bathed her hands and respectfully painted" in neat writing, and then comfortably lay in the round chair.

"I really like this painting, sister, I love the willow branch in her hand the most."

"That is to save people from the suffering of the world."

"What about those who have neither suffering nor happiness?"

"Then, ah, then, - then they should endure it well!"

Qingsong said faintly, like someone who had already escaped from the world, her eyes fixedly gazing out the window at the swaying poplar tree in the autumn wind.

"Let me play a tune."

Qingzhi said, taking down the xiao hanging on the wall.

"I'm afraid that my sister will feel tired again."

"No, I'm very happy, let me play a section of Zhaojun's Lament, okay?"

Qingzhi tried to blow it twice, and sat down on the chair near the window, her thin figure, like an old man in his twilight years, the slow and low sound of the xiao, slowly rose.

This was completely in great silence, almost even breathing stopped, in the sound of the xiao, one could find the sorrow that was difficult to make up for throughout the ages, and one could imagine such a beautiful woman, lonely and unhappy, shedding tears there, with the wind blowing south outside the tent. She envied that the grass could turn green every year, she also envied that the birds with wings could fly to the places they wanted to go, but she herself, had to spend this life in cold loneliness.

While playing, Qingzhi's eyes were gradually covered with a layer of tears, she tried to endure it, and widened her eyes even more; but the tears flowed itchily from her cheeks.

Yarn and Cotton

Reduced Working Hours May Lead to Increased Yarn Prices

The yarn market is trending stronger, with rising prices becoming more intense. Due to previously pessimistic views on the market outlook, general retail investors were selling off, so a positive news triggered a more drastic rebound. Today, manufacturers, in order to maintain their factories, convened a meeting of various factories at 3 PM to discuss ways to unite. The general idea is to cooperate to maintain the yarn market, and potentially reduce working hours. As a result, the news spread, short sellers actively covered their positions, and buying surged. According to some investigations, foreign firms were said to have sold off more than 30,000 bales in the standard market, so old standard yarns may see another drastic change.

Hunan Province to Clear Existing Yarn Stock

More than 6,000 pieces of accumulated yarn

No goods will be processed until cleared

Changsha, Hunan has more than 6,000 pieces of 20-count and 16-count cotton yarn in stock. Sales are sluggish. On the 8th of this month, the Hunan Provincial Cotton Yarn Management Office held its first joint meeting with merchants, chaired by Director Yang Boheng. The following resolutions were passed: (1) For the 16-count and 20-count cotton yarns, the Management Office will notify all merchants to temporarily suspend the processing of import goods from today (the 8th). After the existing stock of the said yarn sells well, a meeting will be convened to discuss other measures. (2) For 16-count and 20-count cotton yarns ordered by yarn merchants from factories in Shanghai and Hankou before the meeting date, but not yet shipped, evidence of the order (such as telegrams and order forms from Shanghai and Hankou) must be submitted to the Management Office for registration by the 10th of this month. Only after the Management Office verifies the authenticity will it be considered valid. Late registrations will not be accepted. (3) For 16-count and 20-count cotton yarns purchased by yarn merchants from factories in Shanghai and Hankou that have already been shipped, all must be transported and imported by the 15th of this month. However, this does not apply to goods for which evidence has been verified by the Management Office and registered, proving that the order was placed before the meeting date; otherwise, registration will not be accepted. (4) For both 20-count and 16-count cotton yarns, the stock accumulated in the city should be promoted first. If the yarn of Brand A of a certain count is sold out, it should be supplemented by the yarn of Brand B of the same count. Without the approval of the second meeting, no goods of the same count of any brand may be ordered from factories in Shanghai and Hankou. (5) During the period of suspension of imports, the prices of 16-count and 20-count yarns in the city should be based on the market prices discussed daily by the Shanghai Yarn Merchants Association based on the Shanghai and Hankou market conditions, and should not be arbitrarily raised or lowered or manipulated. (6) If any of the above articles are violated, the Management Office will investigate and store all of the yarn and resolve the matter at the second joint meeting.

US Cotton Stagnant, No Distinctive Features

Yesterday's US cotton market was stagnant and lacked distinctive features. Traders were adopting a wait-and-see attitude. The market initially rose due to positive news from Liverpool, but then fell back due to selling from the South. As a result, spot prices fell by 5 points and futures prices fell by 1 point to 4 points. Liverpool spot cotton rose by 5 points and futures rose by 6 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices remained unchanged. The Bombay cotton market initially fell due to profit-taking by bulls and selling by speculators, but then rebounded as short sellers covered their positions. As a result, Pingar rose by 2 rupees and 2.5 annas, Omra rose by 1.5 rupees, and Bailoxi rose by 1 rupee. The original telegram is recorded on the left (telegram of the 13th).

Grain Industry Outside Short Covering for Near-Term Flour

Yesterday's flour market saw a initially flat and then improving trend in the morning across various months. As foreign wheat quotations in Chicago and Canada were down approximately two to three cents, the opening prices were soft. Later, because factories continued to refuse to sell and outside short positions gradually moved to cover, sentiment was lifted as there was more buying than selling. The afternoon opening continued to show improvement, and although trading wasn't very active, short positions continued to cover smoothly. Major factories intended to maintain prices and didn't offer any product, further boosting sentiment. However, northern merchants were still selling due to inactive sales. As a result, the current month was up 1.5 cents from the previous day, April was up 1.25 cents, May, June, and July were up 2 cents, and August was down 1.5 cents.

Near-Term Wheat Suddenly Drops Seven to Eight Cents

Yesterday, the futures wheat market showed a sharp decline in the near term, while the far term was stable. Foreign wheat prices in Chicago and Canada were down approximately two to three cents, but investor sentiment hadn't fully focused on it. Later, the market suddenly received a stimulus, likely due to the fact that prices couldn't be pushed up further. The squeezed gains of the current month, initially due to a lack of goods, saw a situation where the primary number offered foreign wheat for delivery, but the bulls became powerless and unanimously gave up. The market suddenly plummeted. The morning opening was 4.1 yuan, and the afternoon offer of 1 yuan was rejected, showing a lack of interest in price increases. Far-term trading was limited, and prices were stable. As a result, the current month plummeted 8 cents from the previous day, April fell 7 cents, and August fell 1 cent. The spot wheat market remained stable and improving, with high-grade goods up another 5 cents. Bengbu wheat opened at 3.61 yuan, Yingzhou wheat at 3.65 yuan, Yaowan wheat at 3.65 yuan, Shandong wheat at 3.68 yuan, and South Suzhou wheat at 3.67 yuan, totaling 2,500 yuan, and was reportedly purchased by Fuxin Huafeng.

Lower Reaches Rice Supply Arrives, Turning Turbulent

Thick粳 Rice Drops Another 5 Cents...Yin Yuan Rice Drops Nearly 10 Cents

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, the sources for various merchants were hindered by the previous days of wind and rain, but arrived in full force yesterday with clear weather. The docks were very crowded, with an estimated 80-90 ships (over 10,000 stones), mostly thick粳 rice and various types of rice. Late rice accounted for nearly 40 ships. Sales-wise, although the appetite of the street shops was relatively strong, the overall situation appeared ordinary after a long period of weakness. Coupled with the sudden surge in supply, an oversupply was almost inevitable. Therefore, the market for common varieties of 粳 rice from the Su, Tong, and South Port merchants was soft, and prices fell by 5 cents. As for the late rice varieties from Qingjiao, Songjiang, Xishi, and Lian merchants, although the supply was also significant, fortunately, both the northern and southern foreign merchants showed strong interest. Therefore, the initial market started off with a slight drop, but until the close, there was no significant decline. A total of 3,400-3,500 packages were taken in, and sellers took the opportunity to call for higher prices. As a result, the market was stable due to the tight buying from the Hakka traders. Du Yangjian’s sales were similar, with no significant gains or losses. The supply of Yin Yuan rice was relatively large, and sales were limited. The market was weak, with prices down by nearly a foot. Bian Yuan rice was scarce, showing a glimmer of hope.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 32-33 ships from various merchants in the lower reaches arrived. There was still some demand for various goods in the market. The price of white 粳 rice and 柆尖 rice fell by nearly 10 cents. High-quality early thin rice was stable, while medium and low-quality rice was also weaker by several cents. Yangbu Kejian, Bai Yuan, and Yin Yuan rice were stable.

Ke Xian Rice Rises by 10 Cents

Merchants from Fujian and Zhejiang Are Very Eager to Buy

Yesterday, the market for Ke Xian rice was initially weak, but Kehua was very popular. The market sentiment was tight, and prices were rising. High and low grades all rose, increasing by 7-8 cents to 12-3 cents compared to the previous market. High-quality goods were particularly scarce, and Hakka merchants were very interested in buying. It is expected that there will be a need for continued buying. Yesterday, Fuzhou had the best demand, buying 1,000 packages of Jiangxi Jiwan rice, 1,000 packages of Hunan Jiyou Jijing rice, 1,000 packages of Mingguang coarse rice, 1,000 packages each of Quanzhou machine-processed red rice and Xuzhou machine-processed Xian rice, 300 packages of coarse red rice, 1,500 packages of Ningbo desalted Shashi coarse rice, 300 packages of Nanjing coarse rice, and 350 packages of Wenzhou machine-processed early rice. More than 400 packages of Ji Cao rice were purchased by local shops, while 50 packages of Wuxi Ji Yuan were purchased by Fuzhou. A total of 7,880 packages were sold. Rice was purchased by merchants from Fujian province, and the markets in Quanzhou and Fuzhou in Fujian province were still interested in buying. It is expected that shipments will continue today and tomorrow, so the market outlook is still promising.

Soybean Market Mediocre

Yesterday's soybean market was active, but actual sales were difficult to develop. Although it was once driven by bean cake sales, the abundance of goods led to lower prices, making it difficult to maintain sentiment. Yesterday's selling prices were not significantly different from the previous market. Factories sold six to seven cars of Yingzhou soybeans, priced from 2.52 yuan to 2.50 yuan. Three cars of Bengbu soybeans were sold at prices ranging from 2.45 yuan to 2.40 yuan. More than 1,000 packages of Dangshan soybeans were sold at prices ranging from 2.52 yuan to 2.48 yuan. In addition, four to five cars of Guide soybeans, Feihe soybeans, and Zhengyangguan soybeans were distributed to the inland and local markets.

Sugar Market Domestic Sliced Green Sugar Arrives in Large Quantities

Yesterday, the Sugar Association's opening price for rough brown and white sugar was still 19.63 yuan, with slight transactions. The prices of Taikoo sugar and local factory's refined sugar were the same as yesterday. Dozens of packages of domestic Double Cover white sugar were opened at a price of 17 yuan. Dried Goods

Jinshan Round Lychees Have Sluggish Sales and Falling Prices

Recently, the supply of Guangdong's Jinshan round lychees has been steadily increasing, while sales have been flat. Therefore, the asking prices have softened again. It was recently heard that Guangdong merchants opened a hundred boxes, with prices dropping by 3-4 yuan compared to before. The higher grades, such as Ruichang brand sun-dried lychees, were only opening at 75 yuan. Chrysanthemum rice, such as all-yellow high-grade rice, had long been sold out and the supply was cut off for a long time, so the market was popular and prices soared. Currently, large-grain, all-yellow, sand-free rice is trading at 40 yuan. Yesterday, it was heard that the dealers received a letter from the producing area stating that shipments had already been made and were expected to arrive soon. It is expected that there will be a situation of insufficient supply at that time.

Oil Market Asphalt Selling Prices Fall Daily

Since asphalt prices have repeatedly fallen in various producing areas, the market has become depressed. Arrivals have gradually increased. Recently, the Han market has seen a drop of 15 yuan per dan for Macheng oil. Few merchants are buying, and supply exceeds demand. Although prices have fallen to this level, which hasn't been seen in years, soap factories still find the prices high and unprofitable. The use for candles is limited, and the accumulation of goods in producing areas such as western Hubei is still high. Therefore, the market trend is still weak. Local merchants, seeing the sluggish spring sales, are unwilling to stock up too much. Due to the arrival of goods, merchants have not yet opened their prices. Selling prices are gradually falling. The price of Ming Chong Jing oil is 20.045 yuan per dan, Ping Jing oil is 20 yuan, and Macheng oil is 18 yuan per dan.

Peanut Oil Deliveries Arrive Continuously

--Sluggish Sales--

The peanut oil market is trending downwards due to the weakness of soybean oil. Recently, supplies have been arriving continuously, and inventories are piling up. Only Zhejiang province still has some transactions, but prices are low. Yesterday the downward trend opened. Compared to last week, prices dropped by 8 cents. A thousand cases of Boer oil were opened at 9 yuan, two thousand cases of Jiacang oil were opened at 8.8 yuan, and two thousand cases of light skin oil were opened at 8.4 yuan.

Silk and Tea

New York Raw Silk Sales Gradually Decreasing

(Less Than 40,000 Bales in the Previous Month) The Shanghai Raw Silk Export Association received a telegram from the New York Silk Association yesterday, stating that although New York silk mills are weaving spring silk fabrics, due to world trends and fashion trends, most are focusing on man-made silk, leading to even lower consumption of raw silk. Last month (February), New York City silk mills consumed only 39,021 bales of raw silk from China, Japan, Italy, and France. Japanese silk accounted for more than 90%, and Chinese silk accounted for less than 1,000 bales, a decrease of 1,933 bales compared to January.

(Silk Filature Long Filaments Supply Slightly Smoother) Wuxi silk filatures are actively reeling silk as spring cocoons are about to hatch. Many who have surplus cocoons are renting filatures to reel silk. As a result, three or four more have started operation since the lunar new year. The production of long silk filaments has gradually increased and the supply is slightly smoother. In the past half-month, Wuxi silk filatures received a total of 86 bales of long silk filaments.

(Comparison of Waste Silk Exports Over Two Years) China's yellow and white silk and silk cocoon waste (referred to as waste silk by customs) also occupy an important position in export goods. Each year, 60-70,000 dan are exported to Europe and the Americas. In recent years, affected by Japanese silk waste (i.e., waste silk) and man-made silk, waste silk exports have plummeted. According to the survey, from June 1, last year to March 10, this year, a total of 19,901 dan of waste silk were exported, compared to 19,259 dan in the same period last year, an increase of 642 dan.

(Filature Ashes Primarily For Short Covering) Silk mills in Europe and America are still reducing consumption of spring silk fabrics, while Japanese silk is being sold aggressively. Sales of Chinese silk filatures have not improved. Shanghai's American banks are primarily engaged in short covering. Lianna and others imported 30 bales of white factory waste and 10 bales of gray waste, and prices remained flat and weak.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Idle Talk

On the Reforestation Movement

— Liu An

In the past, our Chinese Arbor Day was on Qingming Day, but now it has been changed to the anniversary of Premier Sun's death, and Arbor Day has been expanded and enlarged to Reforestation Movement Day. This is a clear symbol of "national rejuvenation." As this national reforestation movement is underway, newspapers have special issues dedicated to the reforestation movement, promoting and encouraging it with a refreshing outlook.

One university professor published an article arguing that the only way to alleviate rural bankruptcy is through reforestation. His argument has approximately three points:

(1) Production increases year by year and is stable.

(2) Reduce the number of farmers running to the cities.

(3) Seek fundamental improvements in water conservancy.

From the above three statements, one can understand the effects of forestry: it can increase and stabilize production, gradually reduce the number of unemployed farmers, and fundamentally improve water conservancy. These three are the most urgent problems to be solved in rural areas. Without seeking increased and stable production, farmers cannot eat their fill and stay warm; without gradually reducing the number of unemployed farmers, farmers become evildoers in society; without fundamentally improving water conservancy, one will inevitably face frequent floods and droughts. Therefore, solving these three major problems is to save the countryside. To completely solve these three major problems, only forestry can succeed. So, in summary, forestry is the only way to save the countryside. Now is the Arbor Day season, hoping everyone will rouse their spirits and work together on reforestation, turning the country's barren mountains and vacant lands completely into forest areas. Saving the nation and ensuring its survival depends on this one move.

This kind of contribution strategy of "saving the nation and ensuring its survival depends on this one move" will naturally be noted by the National Government; if the Rural Reconstruction Committee also adopts this suggestion as a resolution, vigorously taking action on forestry to save and revive the countryside, then "saving the nation and ensuring its survival" may be successful. However, we dare not fully agree. May I ask, in the country's mountainous areas, such as the total area of 567,133,003,689 mu surveyed by the Ministry of Statistics in the 18th year of the Republic, are they all barren mountains and vacant lands without forests? Every year, countless farmers rely on the trees (such as mulberry trees, fruit trees, etc.) and agricultural products of those mountainous areas for their livelihood. However, the products of mountainous areas, like the products of fields, must be taxed. If farmers want to engage in forestry, may I ask, some mountain lands are government property and some are privately owned by large landlords. Where do farmers get the money to rent or buy mountain land for reforestation? If large landlords are encouraged to engage in forestry, naturally "in lean years," they can "engage in forest work, either planting, felling, transporting, or manufacturing" in their forest land to profit. However, it is difficult to say whether farmers "can be accommodated as much as possible" to work. Moreover, in the current sluggish market for timber, even if large landlords regard forests as a major product and hire farmers to fell them, they may not be able to profit. Once large landlords calculate the balance, no one wants to do this loss-making business. Then, even if the country's barren mountains and vacant lands are widely forested, where can farmers find work to do, and how can the number of unemployed farmers gradually decrease? Then, what is meant by "forestry is the only way to save the countryside"? The so-called "saving the nation and ensuring its survival depends on this one move," I am afraid the reasons are not sufficient.

However, reforestation is a fundamental way to manage water conservancy, which should be supported and promoted to observe its success.

Originally... "His Frustration?"

— Fu

These past few days, friends have seen that Aji's expression is very negative and decadent. He's mentally distracted and listless. His attitude has also changed a lot. He—is too lazy to move anything, and his behavior and actions are completely different from what they were a month ago. Sometimes, he's just seen pacing alone, sighing frequently with furrowed brows. It seems that there is something difficult to tell people on his mind. Originally, living in this society, the kind of distress that young people feel is nothing more than the issue of career prospects. However, for someone like Aji, who has a suitable job and a good environment, and whose family burden is not too heavy, such distress is always considered incomprehensible.

One day, Lao Zhang and I finished watching a movie and wanted me to check on his recent condition. We walked into his bedroom and saw him sitting idly on a chair, staring blankly at the sky.

So, Lao Zhang gently asked him from behind.

"Hey! Aji! What's been up these past few days?"

"Oh! Fine... Haven't seen you in days. Where did you come from?" He replied, seemingly startled by the sudden voice from behind, while also displaying a forced smile.

"We came specially to visit, to visit you."

"Thank you, thank you."

"What have you been doing for amusement lately?"

"Nothing. Sitting around, too lazy to move. I don't feel interested in anything. Anyway, wasting time like this, I think it's very worthwhile," he said, sighing heavily.

Lao Zhang wanted to ask why he was so negative and lazy, hoping that he would say it, or that friends could offer him some mental comfort. So he asked again:

"May I ask you, how is Miss Yong lately? I heard that your love is very passionate, and I imagine it will soon become a reality!"

"Don't mention it. I hate women to the extreme. Because of women, I've become so negative. Miss Yong is engaged to another man. After all, women flow like water. Who can love each other like this forever?" He shrugged, expressing infinite sadness. "Alas! Four or five years of friendship and love can change. No wonder Aji's negativity is an inevitable fact," I said sympathetically.

"Ah! So his frustration is a broken heart," Lao Zhang finally understood. (Unpaid)

About Crying

— Lie Huo

Humans are artistic, and in terms of actions, thoughts, appearance, and inner feelings, there are plenty of laughable and highly artistic elements. For example, "crying," this expression of inner feelings, is a good example. Talking slowly about it is enough to make an article of about a thousand words.

When a baby bids farewell to the womb and lands with a "cry," some people say that it is the first cry of "life's pain." Why not another expression first? Although it is said to be a natural instinct, it is actually close to this kind of "pain theory." This "cry" is a manifestation of true feelings, so it is often recalled and yearned for by older people. However, people will still "cry" when they grow up.

In old China, five- or six-year-old girls were about to grow braids and bind their feet. Although there were many harms in growing braids, the pain seemed unspeakable. Only foot binding was a uniquely female "pain" that no one could deny. Everyone who was bound cried. But no matter how much you cried to heaven and earth, feet had to be bound at that time.

Boys also had a kind of "cry," which was when they attended private schools and began studying, and they were always crying. This kind of crying was a little bit like making it clear that it was soy sauce, and it was also a simple snapshot of education in the past China.

Growing up a bit more, it was different again. For example, when some relatives died, the younger female generation mostly cried very vigorously, especially at the memorial service. When the ritualist shouted to express grief, the women cried out in unison, almost like a musical team. This kind of crying was inevitably a bit mechanical and hypocritical. Another scene that could not be avoided was when getting married, on a colorful sedan chair covered with flowers, there was no one who did not tear up, crying so humorously. Why did they cry? Only the bride herself knew.

On the men's side, there were also people who cried and times when they cried. For example, a pale-faced scholar had taken exams for many years. Every time, he felt that his article was very well written, but often someone reached the age of sixty and still had not obtained a red hat. At this time, it is said that in addition to looking up at the roof and sighing, scolding the examiners for not having eyes, they also cried bitterly that their ancestral graves were not effective. Another was a wife who only knew how to give birth to girls, and the concubine who was added to the family was also the same. Then, thinking of the lack of successors, they could not help but cry loudly and specially.

The above counts as various kinds of crying in the old era and old society. Speaking of today's new society, crying is still just as popular. New-style ladies have several ways of crying. For example, when they lose love or their husbands die, they often cry very fiercely. But in the midst of crying, they often receive the love of new lovers. Perhaps this is why new-style women are new. Their emotional seeds are so turbulent, crying easily occurs and easily disappears. Most of the time, when they want to coerce something in front of their husbands and cannot achieve their goal, using the "crying" trick has the hope of a satisfactory solution. This counts as their "crying coquetry." Or, the person they married is not suitable, but they themselves are so delicate, and the man is a country bumpkin. It is inevitable to cry behind people's backs that a phoenix has followed a crow. Or, discovering in the mirror that their youth has faded, and that the standards for choosing a partner in the past were too harsh, the men who are pursuing them are gradually becoming scarce. On lonely nights, they must cry painfully.

We cannot see any meaning in these. Only the crying of women during childbirth because they cannot bear the pain of childbirth is truly great and worthy of praise.

Speaking of ordinary young gentlemen, they also love to cry like people in the old era, but what they cry about is slightly different. For example, crying for lost love is the most common cry among young people. Some even cry while in love. Not getting a doctorate or master's degree, or being unemployed and drifting around, does not cause them to cry. What "national crisis" is even less likely to arouse a trace of "crying." Even if there is crying, it is fake, to gain fame and seek praise. It seems that I only read in the newspaper that some adult gentleman "cried with a choked voice" during a speech. That was certainly crying...

I feel that crying is a bit mysterious and meaningless. Even if it is an unavoidable expression of humans, I also think that real "crying" and real tears should be for the masses of humanity. Furthermore, what we expect is that humans should not have crying or tears, only strength and blood.

To Those Who Cry for Ai Xia

— Zhi

Ai Xia has been dead for quite some time. Many newspapers and magazines have published several special issues to commemorate her "life" and "death," and the writers who admired her have shed countless compassionate tears. Furthermore, her death has stimulated the feelings of some young men and women in Shanghai society, questioning the causes and consequences of Ai Xia's suicide, and similarly exploring what life is all about!

I am very surprised that Ai Xia's death is more sensational to society than her life, because I have seen many people die—suicide, death from illness, death from hunger and cold, wrongful death (including bloody death). I don't know how many men, women, old, and young die like this every day, but they all die without leaving a shadow on society, and no one has held a memorial service for him or her in newspapers and magazines. Why is Ai Xia's death different from ordinary people?

Here, I want to ask those writers who "write with tears" to commemorate Ai Xia, and the editors of those newspapers and magazines, are you crying and writing about Ai Xia's death because she is a person in the arts, she is a contemporary star, and she is a modern beauty? If this is the case, it is a romantic mood of pitying the flower and cherishing the jade that is set into motion in the heart; creating articles and compiling publications, such things are of no benefit to the dead or to society.

A person's death, no matter what, should be sympathized with. Ai Xia's death is naturally one that people should sympathize with. Living people should bear responsibility for death: natural death and artificial death, or suicide and death by others. This is also a matter of reason. Here, I want to ask those who cry for Ai Xia again, do you cry for other dead people with the same tears?

Today's world is indeed suffering from a great calamity, and everyone is living and struggling bitterly. If they cannot live or cannot survive, some people are willing to die. Recently, many people have been discussing the issue of suicide, and everyone is only groping for the reasons, but cannot find a way to prevent suicide. The reason for not finding a way is that society does not have a force to prevent suicide from arising, that is, society does not have a band of connection with each other, and people are all scattered and indifferent.

In this human world with scattered and indifferent relationships, the band of connection for survival has been cut off. If we look up at the dead on the Bund, most of them are without help and without relatives, so that they have lost their belief in survival and have to die with hatred. Furthermore, inferring from those heroic spirits who died for lost love, the reason why these people must die is that this society does not have a suitable thing for him or her to develop in another direction. An empty and melancholic life, if you don't seek death, why stay in the world?

In front of us, this realistic society, the misery of survival has reached its peak. There is no connection between people, and even human virtues, righteousness, etc., have all disappeared. The great drama of struggling and tragic fighting makes many people with rich emotions and lofty ideals unwilling to live in this world in a perfunctory manner.

Discussing the issue of suicide, if we want to propose effective ways to prevent suicide, we can only strive to restore the band of connection for human survival, so that people are related to each other and feel each other's pain, and everyone is full of energy and embraces an ideal of noble human life. To put it concretely, that is, to strive to transform the real society and realize a new social life.

All these words, in the final analysis, require a force, which is how to create a force that leads society forward.

Many people focus on expressing themselves in a negative way and then it's over. This is the biggest crisis. Several articles have told the story of Ai Xia's life and death in detail, praising her courage and praising her extraordinariness. Doing so is tantamount to encouraging those who have the intention to commit suicide to covet this posthumous honor, and those who write these articles have unintentionally become teachers of suicide.

There is no need to cry and commemorate Ai Xia's death. Moreover, I believe that this is because of the numbness and indifference of social public opinion that such a thing has happened!

I do not sympathize with Ai Xia's death. I only feel that the cutting off of the band of connection for human survival is a painful thing. I hope that social public opinion will no longer be so numb and indifferent from now on.

The Failure of the First Social Encounter

— Bo Er

Girl, I love your simplicity. You came back from Shanghai. How come the prosperity didn't taint you? This is why I admire you! He leaned against the train door! Facing me, in the rumbling sound of the train, I heard him say that. I thought he wouldn't say such a strange sentence, because at that time, I was indeed wearing a very plain cloth gown, so I didn't think he had other intentions, and I didn't understand that what he said was a way to get acquainted and please people. Although he had been introduced to me once by someone else before. But without direct conversation, this time on the train was an unexpected encounter.

Back home, I didn't remember this incident. The next morning, a postman came outside, not to deliver a letter, but a bulky package. I thought who would send me a gift in this rural place? The appearance of the thing was rectangular, and before opening it, I guessed several parts, knowing that it was books. Sure enough, he sent me four famous novels. This is good, from this time on, I broke the bad habit of not liking to read books. After that, he continued to send them to me, and I could receive almost fifty Chinese and foreign masterpieces within a month. This forced me to feel very embarrassed and very afraid that he would write to me to discuss the issues in the books, then I wouldn't be able to answer, wouldn't it be too embarrassing? So I also used a method to encourage myself, arranging all the books on the table in front of the bed, limiting myself to reading several books every few days. This slowly cultivated my habit of reading.

Naturally, he gave me sincere guidance. In the correspondence, he never talked about emotional matters from beginning to end. He made my heart quiet. I was happy that he gave me a path to learning. I accepted every book he sent me, treating him as my own brother, or rather, as a teacher!

Not long after, I was staying at my aunt's house in Nanjing, and he came to invite me to go to Hangzhou to stroll around. At the time, I also planned to stay at an old classmate's place for a few days, so I agreed to go with him.

The train arrived in Hangzhou in the afternoon. We wanted to find a hotel to tidy up our clothes, wash our faces, and eat something before seeing friends. But after a short rest, he said, "It's time for dinner, wouldn't it be embarrassing to find people? It's better to go early tomorrow morning. I'll get you an extra room!"

The next day, I took a small suitcase and took a rickshaw to my friend's place. But looking at the address, the people in the house were not the people I knew. This surprise made my heart panic. Standing at someone else's door, looking for a long time, there was no way but to return to the hotel with him. At this time, I felt that the hotel was a terrible place, and I dared not stay there any longer. I was very resentful in my heart that I had come to the wrong place. So I sat in a corner without saying a word, and he gently persuaded me to go for a walk. I don't know how long after, I found myself sitting on a small boat, circling the Lake Heart Pavilion, moving back and forth, which seemed to make me dizzy and very comfortable.

That night, I couldn't sleep, because I had never opened a hotel with a man before. I felt like I had committed a crime and felt uncomfortable. I wanted to go back to Shanghai, but I was afraid that I would not be able to catch the train to Nanjing. Stay another night? This night was too difficult for me, and I didn't trust him; although we were staying in different rooms.

Melancholy filled my heart, maybe he was the opposite of me! For dinner, he excitedly drank some wine. I found that his eyes were already emitting an unusual gleam. His unceasing gaze was slanting on my body. He didn't say anything. The air in the room was serious and terrible at this moment. This silence made me tremble. My pure and peaceful soul was startled by him. He really pounced on me and said: "Sister, my heart is burning! You should promise...?" He hugged me tightly and wanted to try to kiss me! Fortunately, the waiter came in at the right time.

Because I was too uncomfortable, I didn't go back to my aunt's place, but took a small car straight home.

"What's going on, why is the house so quiet? Did everyone go out?" I asked the little maid, but she didn't answer. My younger sisters and brothers ran out to look at me and ran back in, which made me panic. I had to bravely step in front of my father's bed. His tiger-like eyes were staring at me and said, "Why are you back?" My mother was tearful and held a letter to show me. It turned out that there were such treacherous men in the world! He wrote a letter telling my father that I had fallen in love with him and had stayed with him in a hotel in Hangzhou.

Forget it, it doesn't count as me being fooled. I packed a few clothes and ran back to Shanghai to find a life for myself elsewhere.

Amateur Mailbox

One Family's Life

Answer: After reading this letter, the editor has two thoughts. First, the gentry's authority in our society is so sought after, the gentry can be considered a "profession," and the gentry can do evil. Second, Mr. Chen feels in his heart that his father should be "eliminated," but on the one hand, he is also glad that his father was able to "get some money" so that he could "enter school to study from a young age," and he praises him for being able to "benefit (?) society—the lives of more than ten people in the family depend on his support." In order to maintain his personal and family life, he wants to prevent and avoid the maid's mother from accusing his father, hoping that his father's sins will be reduced, and he can no longer act according to his conscience. Therefore, while the editor admires Mr. Chen's frankness and sincerity, and forgives his difficulties, he also feels the greatness of the power of the living environment in determining people's actions.

Mr. Chen is afraid that once his father is accused by the maid's mother, he will not escape the law. In fact, this is entirely the fantasy of a young man with a pure heart who has not seen much of the world, and it is an unnecessary fear. No wonder your father will not listen to your advice. Why? Mr. Chen's father is a "gentleman" who can support a family of more than ten people by relying on the "gentleman" profession, then the "authority" and "usefulness" of the "gentleman" can also be clearly seen. Therefore, his old man "taking a maid as a concubine" is something he can do in his position. Conversely, if he does not dare or cannot "take a maid as a concubine," or cannot "actually commit the crime of adultery with a young girl," then he is simply not qualified to be a gentleman. Readers and Mr. Chen, seeing the editor's argument, will definitely find it too extreme and will immediately ask: "That's right: the gentry has power, but why does the maid's mother still dare to make a fuss? Why doesn't Mr. Chen's father use his gentry power to suppress her?" Then the editor can answer him like this: the situation the editor is talking about originally refers to the general situation in reality, and exceptions are of course inevitable, so this cannot be observed mechanically. However, even in Mr. Chen's situation, according to the editor's speculation, the reason why the maid's mother is so arrogant is not that Mr. Chen's father has no power, or that he is muddleheaded and perfunctory. The biggest reason is that Mr. Chen's father is infatuated with the maid, and at the same time has ill feelings towards your old mother. Therefore, the maid's mother dares to be so bold and dares to make "outrageous" demands. Mr. Chen, look, if your father is no longer confused by the maid's mother in the future, will her mother dare to make such a fuss—Mr. Chen didn't say that his father is somewhat intelligent and capable, and has also worked as a teacher and a politician, so how could he be so confused that he doesn't even understand this little bit of legal knowledge? So, the reason why he dares to be so bold and reckless is that he has something to rely on and has no fear. Isn't the maid now subdued under "his lewd power"? If her mother really dares to oppose your father, why doesn't she sue him now, but comes to make a mess with your mother and others? From this point of view, even if her mother is extremely greedy and fierce, she can't do anything to your father. However, people get desperate and will do anything. In the future, she may sue your father, but you don't need to worry too much about this. If your father's gentry title remains the same, it will be nothing more than spending a little more money to settle the matter. "Crime" and "jail" are definitely out of the question; you can rest assured.

Therefore, what you should study is "what attitude your mother, brothers, wives, etc. should take towards her." Other than that, nothing else becomes a problem. You want to prevent her from making trouble again in the future, which is not successful, and it also commits the fault of "only seeing yourself and not caring about others." Your father ruined someone else's daughter, forcing her to submit under his lewd power, and raping her. This kind of inhumane behavior is probably something even robbers would not do, but in fact, it comes from the hands of noble and graceful gentry. Moreover, people are used to it and are not surprised by this kind of incident at all. On the contrary, they are very surprised, blame, and hate the maid's mother's noise, doing everything possible. The social situation is like this, it is truly lamentable! Mr. Chen's heart is very frank, but because his own interests are too important, he did not say a fair word for her mother, but instead has some resentment. This kind of intention is certainly not a crime for Mr. Chen, but we do not want Mr. Chen to continue to hold this attitude. Other people's daughters are raped by your father, but they should not speak up. You are insulted by her, so you should complain. How can there be such a reason in the world—therefore, the editor regards the maid's mother's resistance as extremely justified, no matter what means she takes. However, the editor believes that her opposition to you is a barbaric act and does not understand the situation, because it is your father who harmed her. She should negotiate with him and come to quarrel with you. It is not only bullying the weak and fearing the strong, but also punishing the innocent. Therefore, the editor believes that Mr. Chen should not speak purely from a personal standpoint, and should not avoid her mother's noise. Instead, he should help her desperately make a big fuss with his father, which is the right thing to do. If Mr. Chen and your mother can take this attitude, it will be beneficial to both people and oneself, and the dispute can be resolved as a result. Otherwise, unless you use a method to suppress her mother so that she does not dare to speak up and submits to your lewd power, there is no way to avoid her making trouble.

The central meaning of Mr. Chen's letter is the problem of life. Therefore, the editor is not at all anxious about what Mr. Chen is extremely anxious about; but on the other hand, the editor is extremely anxious about what Mr. Chen is not very anxious about. There were originally three stores in Mr. Chen's family. Because of the bankruptcy of the countryside and the decline of commerce in recent years, the larger one in the city "closed down during the end of last year!" This should be a very terrible thing! If the economic crisis deepens day by day in the future, and Mr. Chen's stores cannot maintain even one, then even if the maid's mother does not accuse your father of his crimes (in fact, even if she accuses him, and he is fairly punished according to the current law, it will not bankrupt your family), bankruptcy is still inevitable. In fact, according to the editor's shallow economic knowledge, our country's economic crisis will definitely deepen day by day. Imperialist aggression is intensifying day by day, and Mr. Chen's father and others still have to rely on the gentry profession for a living. How can this prevent the countryside from becoming increasingly bankrupt and commerce from declining day by day! The income of Mr. Chen's family has probably decreased compared to before in recent years, but your father still has to "take a maid as a concubine" and spend more money. Therefore, on the one hand, the source of income is less, and on the other hand, more flows out. In this way, even if the remaining two stores do not close down, if the business is not good, then the economy of your family will definitely be very tight. If the harvest of your family's fields at this time is not as good as in previous years, then under the current situation of dumping of foreign rice and cheap grain hurting farmers, your family's economy will accelerate to bankruptcy. In the process of the collapse of the rural economy, the lives of people with land will become a problem, and those landless tenant farmers and hired laborers will be reduced to hunger and cold. When they have no way to go, they will definitely take risks at all costs. At that time, can your father's "gentry profession life" not be shaken? Wouldn't the lives of more than ten people in your family still be without security? However, this is impossible to save.

After Mr. Chen hears the editor's above passage, he should not be too afraid and feel the danger of his own decline. It should be known that fear is useless, and fear cannot avoid the coming of danger. Only by recognizing the nature of the danger and studying how individuals can avoid being harmed by the danger is the only way to avoid danger. Editor

My younger brother is a clever little trickster. The little trickster wants to avenge Lili.

Novel

Lulu's Victory (10) (1)

— Translated by Jingxin, written by M. Saggio, Italy

"I am willing to wait," Lulu replied, "I need to know Robert better."

In fact, this daughter was observing, she ran around like usual, singing, laughing, and playing mischievously like usual, but she often interrupted these happy behaviors and pondered over her sister. I was carefully listening to every word of Robert's. Her sister often pressed her lips, tightened her eyebrows, and showed a very attentive expression.

Therefore, Lulu looked at her; and strange things happened to her. Robert was also not as calm and happy as before, but rather thoughtful, pale, and excited. He spoke absentmindedly and simply; the things that were very interesting to him before now seemed indifferent; sometimes it took a lot of effort for him to restrain himself and become like before, but only for a very short time. He was not used to pretending, and he did not do it well; his desires and inner pain were displayed in his eyes.

In the meantime, Sophia also showed a different appearance; Sophia, who was always nervous and restless, would sometimes embrace her sister enthusiastically, and sometimes would not look at her for several hours, hiding from her. A dark red tide, a fiery red tide, appeared on her cheeks; a flame burned in her eyes; her voice was now heavy and full of emotion, hoarse and grating; her hands trembled. She did not sleep at night. Lulu often got up at night, walked barefoot to her door and listened quietly, and heard Sophia tossing and turning in bed and crying. If asked, Sophia would claim that there was no such thing; she always answered the same way. When Sophia and Robert met—which happened every day—the changes that took place in both of them were even more obvious. They spoke very little, answered too abruptly and vaguely, and often had strange glances; often they did not talk all night, but everyone was carefully studying each other's every move. They never sat together; but Robert always found an excuse to pick up the needlework and books that Sophia had touched. Sometimes when she was not in the house, Robert became more and more uneasy, staring at the closed door, answering people's questions absentmindedly. Sometimes Sophia had only been there for five minutes when he picked up his hat and said goodbye. This daughter became pale, with two dark circles under her eyes. Finally, she decided not to let people see her. For about a week, she locked herself in the house every night, trembling intolerably, trying to suppress her unhappiness.
